@01

GLENG GZHI,

BOD RIGS NI RANG RGYAL GYI LO RGYUS YUN RING LDAN PA'I MI RIGS
RLABS CHEN ZHIG YIN

LA, LAS LA BRTZON ZHING DPA' BA DANG, BLO RIG LDAN PA ZHIG
KYANG RED, RLABS CHEN GYI

MES RGYAL GSAR GTOD BYED PA'I GO RIM NANG DU BYAS RJES 'OD
STONG 'BAR BA BZHAG YOD

CING, LO RGYUS 'PHEL RGYAS KYI CHU KLUNG RING PO 'DI'I NANG DU
BOD KYI MI RIGS DANG MI RIGS

GZHAN DAG THUN MONG THOG NAS MES RGYAL GYI RIG GZHUNG 'OD
STONG RAB TU 'PHRO BA ZHIG GSAR

GTOD BYAS YOD PA RED, BOD YIG GI DPE RNYING 'DI DAG NI MES
RGYAL MI RIGS KYI RIG

GZHUNG GI NOR MDZOD NANG GI MU TIG GZI 'OD RAB TU 'PHRO BA
ZHIG RED,

BOD YIG GI DPE RNYING DE DAG DUS RABS BCU GCIG PA'I GONG LA
SANGS RGYAS KYI

GSUNG RAB BSGYUR RGYU DE GTZO BOR BYAS SHING, DE NI BOD KYI
BTZAN PO MES DBON RNAM

GSUM GYI DUS NAS 'GO TSUGS PA ZHIG RED, BTZAN PO KHRI SRONG
LDE BTZAN GYI SKABS SU

BSGYUR ZIN PA'I GSUNG RAB THAMS CAD DKAR CHAG TU BKOD PA
'PHANG THANG MA DANG, MCHIMS

PHU MA, LDAN DKAR MA GSUM YOD RUNG 'PHANG MCHIMS GNYIS KYI
DKAR CHAG 'THOR GYAR DU

SONG BAS LDAN DKAR MA TZAM LAS MA LUS PA DE NI BSTAN 'GYUR GYI
SNA TSOGS ZHES PA'I KHROD

DU BZHUGS PA 'DI YIN, DKAR CHAG 'DI'I NANG BKA' BSTAN GNYIS
SDE TSAN BCU DGUR

PHYES TE THEG CHEN DANG, THEG DMAN, MDO PHYOGS, SNGAGS PHYOGS,
SDE SNOD GSUM BCAS

KYI GO RIM LTAR PHYE THOG MDO SDE'I SDE SNOD NANG PHAR PHYIN
DANG, PHAL CHEN, DKON BRTZEGS,

BSDUS PA CHEN PO BCAS KYI GO RIM LTAR BSGRIGS 'DUG DE NI GSUNG
RAB SDE TSAN DBYE

BA'I SROL THOG MAR GTOD PA ZHIG RED,

BOD LA SANGS RGYAS CHOS LUGS DAR BA DANG CHABS CIG CHOS LUGS
GRUB MTHA' 'DRA

MIN 'GA' RE BYUNG BA'I 'GO TSUGS SHING, DUS RABS BCU GCIG PA
TSUN TZAM LA GSUNG

RAB DE DAG GI DGONGS 'GREL DANG, LO RGYUS, SKAD YIG RIG GNAS
SKOR SOGS KYI RTZOM

@02

RIGS JE MANG DU PHYIN TE RTZOM RIGS KYI GLEGS BAM HA CANG MANG
PO ZHIG DAR BA RED, DE

DAG NI BOD YIG GI DPE RNYING NANG GI GRUB CHA GAL CHEN ZHIG
RED, NANG DON MDOR BSDUS NA

RIG GNAS CHE BA LNGA STE BZO RIG PA DANG, GSO BA RIG PA, SGRA
RIG PA, GTAN TSIGS

RIG PA, NANG DON RIG PA BCAS DANG, RIG GNAS CHUNG BA LNGA STE
SNYAN NGAG DANG, MNGON

BRJOD, SDEB SBYOR, ZLOS GAR, SKAR RTZIS BCAS YOD PA RED, LHAG
PAR DU LO RGYUS DANG

RNAM THAR SKOR GYI RTZOM RIGS MANG TZAM ZHIG YOD PA DE'I NANG
NAS BSTAN RTZIS RE'U MIG DANG,

RGYAL RABS, MI RIGS BAR GYI 'BREL BA'I SKOR GYI LO RGYUS, CHOS
'BYUNG, GRUB MTHA' SO

SO'I BLA RGYUD, GDUNG RABS, RANG RNAM, GSANG BA'I RNAM THAR
SOGS DANG, GNAS YIG

DANG, DGON PA'I GDAN RABS SOGS YOD PAR MA ZAD, GZHAN YANG MGUR
MA DANG,

LEGS BSHAD, TSIGS SPEL MA'I SNYAN NGAG GI GTAM RGYUD SOGS
KYANG YOD LA, GNA' DUS

RGYA GAR GYI SKAD YIG SAm SKRi TA'I SGRA RIG PA DANG, GTAN
TSIGS RIG PA, SNYAN NGAG SOGS

GSAL BSHAD BYED PA'I MCHAN 'GREL SKOR GYI RTZOM RIGS KYANG MI
NYUNG BA ZHIG YOD PA RED,

DE DAG KHYON YONGS KYI GRANGS 'BOR JI TZAM YOD PA NI RE RE
BZHIN BRJOD KYIS MI LANG NGO, ,

GONG GSAL RIG GNAS SHUL BZHAG 'DI DAG NI BOD KYI SANGS RGYAS
CHOS LUGS DANG BOD

RIGS KYI RIG GZHUNG LA BRTAG DPYAD BYED RGYUR BLANGS NA RDZOGS
RGYU MED PA DANG SPYAD NA

'DZAD MTHA' MED PA'I BANG MDZOD CIG YIN PAS RANG CAG GIS BRTZI
MTHONG CHEN PO BYED

'OS PA ZHIG RED,

GSUNG 'BUM SKOR GYI RTZOM RIGS NI BKA' BSTAN 'GYUR GYI KHONGS
SU MA GTOGS

PA'I DPE RNYING RTZOM RIGS KYI GRUB CHA GTZO BO ZHIG YIN LA
BOD YIG DPE RNYING GI BCUD LTA

BU RED, DUS RABS BCO BRGYAD PA'I MJUG LA KLONG RDOL BLA MA
NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG GIS

TSAN DPE THO ZHIB PHRA TZAM

PA'I DKYIL LA

THO BKOD 'DUG

BOD RIGS KYI RIG GNAS BYA GZHAG SHUL 'DZIN DANG DAR SPEL BYED
RGYU DANG, MI

RIGS KHAG GI RIG GNAS BRJE RES BYED RGYU, THUN MONG DU DAR
RGYAS PHUN SUM TSOGS PA YONG

BAR SKUL SPEL GTONG RGYU, MI RIGS KYI TSAN RIG ZHIB 'JUG GI
BYA BA BYED RGYU, DNGOS PO

DANG BSAM BLO'I DPAL YON GNYIS KYI 'DZUGS SKRUN BYED RGYU BCAS
LA ZHABS 'DEGS ZHU BA'I

CHED DU 'DI GA DPE MDZOD KHANG GI BOD YIG DPE RNYING LEGS
SGRIG BYED PA'I RMANG GZHI'I THOG

'DI GAR BZHUGS YOD PA'I BOD YIG DPE RNYING NANG GSUNG 'BUM
SKOR GYI DKAR CHAG ZHIB

PHRA BSGRIGS NAS, THOG MAR DEB 'DI BSGRIGS PA YIN, DEB 'DI'I
NANG KHYON BSDOMS

MKHAS DBANG BRGYA DANG BRGYAD CU TZAM GYI GSUNG 'BUM 'DUS YOD
CING, DEB GSUM DU

BGOS TE RIM PAS PAR BSKRUN BYED RGYU YIN, GSUNG 'BUM SKOR GYI
DKAR CHAG 'DI NI DPE

CHA DANG DPYAD GZHI SOGS 'TSOL BDE CHED BOD RGYA SKAD GNYIS
SHAN SBYAR BYAS NAS BKOD YOD

PA'I LAG CHA LTA BU'I DEB CIG YIN, 'ON KYANG 'DI GA'I DPE
MDZOD KHANG DU YOD PA'I DPE

CHA'I GNAS TSUL MTSON PA TZAM ZHIG LAS, BOD YIG DPE RNYING
NANG GSUNG 'BUM SKOR GYI

RTZOM RIG YOD DO COG GI RNAM PA YONGS SU MTSON MI THUB,

BOD YIG DPE RNYING RNAMS LA DPE MING RGYAS PA DANG BSDUS PA
GNYIS YOD CING, DPE

MING RGYAS PA DE DAG HA CANG RING BAS BLOR NGES DKA' BA DANG,
LHAG PAR DU THUN MONG MA

YIN PA'I KHYAD CHOS DMIGS BSAL RE YOD LA, THA SNYAD DANG MNGON
BRJOD RNAM GRANGS MANG

BAS KLOG PA POS GO DKA' BA ZHIG DANG, DPE MING KHA BYANG BSDUS
PA DE DAG NI MING 'DRA BA

MANG BAS DKAR CHAG BZO DUS RNYOG 'DZING YONG SLA BA ZHIG RED,
DER BRTEN DPE CHA'I KHA

BYANG YONGS RDZOGS JI BZHIN BSHUS NAS DKAR CHAG BZOS YOD,

NGA TSOS CHED DMIGS KYIS RTZOM PA PO SO SO'I GNAS TSUL MDOR
BSDUS RE NGO SPROD ZHUS

NI YAB TSE MGON RGYAL DANG YUM HAL CAN

KHU'AM BOD MING BLO BZANG NYI MA GNYIS LA SRAS BZHI DANG SRAS MO
BZHI STE MING SRING BRGYAD YOD PA'I NANG GI CHE

SHOS YIN, RAB BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I LCAGS PHO SPREL GYI LO (1740)
ZLA BA BRGYAD PA'I TSES GSUM NYIN PAR SKU

BLTAMS, BYIS PA LO GNYIS TZAM NAS MES MO'I GUR DU SKYED SRING
BYED SKABS GRIB NAD BZHES TE ZHAL DANG

SHANGS 'KHYOG POR GYUR KYANG RING PO MA LON PAR DVANGS TE RGYUN
LDAN DU GYUR, DGUNG LO BDUN PAR PHEBS PA NA,

AA KHU DGE TSUL ZHIG YOD PA DE'I MDUN THOG MAR SOG YIG DANG DE
NAS BOD YIG GZAB GSHAR SOGS SBYANGS,

LO DER CHAS PA BLO BZANG 'PHRIN LAS KYI DRUNG NAS RAB TU BYUNG
ZHING DGE BSNYEN GYI SDOM PA ZHUS, MING BLO BZANG

TSUL KHRIMS ZHES PA BTAGS, GZHAN PHAN BYANG CHUB GLING GI DGON
PAR TSOGS SU ZHUGS, LO MANG RING AA KHU

DGE RGAN DU BSTEN NAS SHES BYA MTHA' DAG 'BAD PAS SBYANGS, DGUNG
LO BCO LNGA PA SHING KHYI LOR, KHONG MING

SRING RNAMS 'BRUM NAG GIS MNAR, AA KHU DANG GCUNG GCIG SRAS MO
GSUM MNYAM DU GRONGS, KHONG BSNYUNG GZHI

SHIN TU LCI BA BZHES KYANG MTHAR 'BRUM NAG LAS THAR, DE NAS MI
RING BAR, AA CHI THU NO MON HAN BLO BZANG

BSTAN 'DZIN DRUNG NAS DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA BZHES, DGUNG LO BCU
BDUN PA ME BYI LOR MTSO BDUN DGON DU

THENGS DANG POR PHEBS, SHES RAB RAB 'BYAMS PA'I MDUN NAS BOD SOG
SGRA SGYUR GYI YON TAN RAGS TZAM

GSAN, DE NAS TSUR PHEBS, RANG DGON DU BLO BZANG DGE LEGS MDUN
SKYABS 'GRO'I KHRID DANG THIG TSAD SBYANGS,

DGUNG LO NYI SHU PA SA MO YOS KYI LO'I DBYAR KHAR MTSO BDUN DGON
DU BYON, KHRI CHEN SPRUL SKU BLO BZANG BSTAN

PA'I NYI MA LAS DGE SLONG GI SDOM PA MNOS, DE NAS GZHAN PHAN
BYANG CHUB GLING DANG MTSO BDUN DGON BCAS SU

GU SHR'I CHOS RJE BLO BZANG RNAM 'PHEL MDUN DU LO 'GA'I BAR
GZHUNG LUGS MANG POR GSAN SBYANGS DANG, ZAB

BA BRGYAD PAR PE CING YUNG HE GUNG DU SLOB

GZHUNG CHEN MO RNAMS LA GSAN SBYONG DANG

BSTEN NAS GZHUNG LUGS MANG POR THOS BSAM

PHAG LO'I ZLA BA DANG PO'I TSES BCO LNGA LA, SLOB DPON BLO BZANG
DAM PA'I MDUN NAS DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA

BZHES, DGUNG LO NYER DRUG PA CHU PHO RTA'I LOR ZLA BA DANG PO'I
TSES BCO LNGA NYIN, NYI MA NUB LA NYE BA'I DUS

SU, RGYA NAG PE CING TZAN DAN JO BO'I LHA KHANG DU, BKA' 'GYUR
BA BLO BZANG TSUL KHRIMS KYIS MKHAN PO DANG,

BYAMS PA LHA KHANG GI CHOS RJE SHES RAB RGYAL MTSAN GYIS GSANG
STON MDZAD DE DGE 'DUN GRANGS TSANG GI DBUS SU

BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI SDOM PA LEGS PAR MNOS, RGYA NAG GONG MAS,
CHINGS SU TZUG THU NO MO HAN ZHES PA'I MTSAN

SNYAN BSTZAL, DGE LDAN BSHAD SGRUB GLING GI BCA' YIG RAB BYUNG
BCU GSUM PA'I ME MO YOS KYI LOR BRTZAMS

PAR BLTAS NA, KHONG NI DGUNG LO SHIN TU GZHON PA'I DUS NAS LHAN
SKYES KYI SHES RAB TSAD MED LDAN PA ZHIG YIN

PAR MNGON, KHONG GI GDAN SA NI SOG YUL GYI DGON PA DGE LDAN

NYIN PAR MDO SMAD TZONG KHA'I YUL GYI BYE BRAG CHU BZANG LUNG

'KHRUNGS, YAB KYIS BKRA SHIS TSE BRTAN ZHES PA'I MING BTAGS,
DGUNG LO BZHI PA LCAGS KHYI LO ZLA BA LNGA PAR

CHE SHOS NGAG DBANG BSTAN PA'I SKU PHRENG DU NGOS 'DZIN BYAS,
BLA MA 'JAM DBYANGS DBANG RGYAL KLOG GI SLOB

GRANGS LNGA PA'I DUS SU, 'JAM BZHAD

'JIGS MED DBANG PO SKU 'BUM DU PHEBS ZHOR CHU RUL KHAR BYON PA
'JAL ZHING CHOS 'BREL 'GA' YANG ZHUS,

DGUNG LO DRUG PAR THU'U BKVAN CHOS KYI NYI MA CHU RUL KHAR
GDAN DRANGS NAS DGE BSNYEN GYI SDOM PA BLANGS TE

GTZUG PHUD PHUL, BLO BZANG BSHAD SGRUB NYI MA ZHES PA'I MING
GNANG, LO DE'I ZLA BA BRGYAD PA'I TSES NYER LNGA

PAR SKU 'BUM DU GDAN DRANGS, SKYA SER MANG POS RING BSU DANG,
DGE 'DUN PA RNAMS KYIS SER SBRENG GZAB

RGYAS KYIS GSUS TE, CHE SHOS BLA BRANG GI BZHUGS KHRIR BKOD,
DGUNG LO DGU PAR MI NYAG TSUL KHRIMS BSTAN

PA'I NYI MA LA RAB BYUNG DANG DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA DKYUS GCIG
TU ZHUS, SKU GONG MA'I MTSAN ZUR NAS DRAS TE,

NGAG DBANG BSHAD SGRUB NYI MA ZHES PA'I MTSAN GSOL, MI NYAG
RIN PO CHE DANG, THU'U BKVAN CHOS KYI NYI MA'I

MDUN RDO RJE 'JIGS BYED SOGS KYI DBANG RJES GNANG 'GA' ZHIG
ZHUS, CHU BZANG RIN PO CHE SKU 'BUM DU

PHEBS NAS 'JIGS BYED DPA' BO GCIG PA'I DBANG GNANG ZHING,
MDZAD SPYOD BZANG ZHING THOS BSAM LA

'BAD DGOS PA'I BSLAB BYA YANG YANG MDZAD, DGUNG LO BCU BZHI

PHEBS, ZLA BA DGU PA'I TSES GNYIS LA DGA' LDAN

DGON NAS MURGE PHYOGS SU GDAN DRANGS, MURGE

DGON SU MU SMON 'PHEL GLING GI DGE 'DUN PA RNAMS KYIS PHEBS
BSU RGYA CHEN MDZAD, 'DU KHANG DU BYON NAS  

KUN LA PHYAG DBANG DANG ZHAL MJAL MDZAD, NYIN GNYIS PA NAS DUS
'KHOR DBANG CHEN BSKUR BA'I STA GON BYAS,

'ON KYANG DBANG YANG STA GON TZAM LA LUS TE ZLA DE'I TSES
BRGYAD PA'I NYIN GUNG GI DUS SU DGONGS PA RDZOGS SO, ,

SGRUB DBANG PHYUG RGYA MTSO, AA KY'A YONGS 'DZIN

RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS NYUNG BSDUS,...

SKU 'BUM KHRI CHEN DON GCIG PA CHE SHOS BLO BZANG BYANG CHUB
BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME NI, MDO SMAD TZONG

KHA'I YUL DU YAB SNGAGS 'CHANG DBANG RGYAL DANG, YUM KA TO GNYIS
KYI SRAS SU, RAB BYUNG BCU BZHI PA'I

LCAGS MO BYA LO'I (1861) ZLA BA DRUG PA'I TSES BZHI'I SNGA DROR
'KHRUNGS, YAB KYIS RIN CHEN DON GRUB CES PA'I

MTSAN GSOL, DGUNG LO GSUM BZHES PA CHU PHAG LO'I ZLA BA DANG
PO'I TSES LNGA LA, DBON CHUNG CHOS RJE 'JAM

DBYANGS CHOS 'PHEL DANG, THAR SHUL RIN PO CHE'I PHYAG MDZOD ZLA
GRAGS SOGS KYIS CHE SHOS GONG MA'I SPRUL SKUR

NGOS 'DZIN, LO DE'I ZLA BA BZHI PA'I TSES BCU GSUM LA, AA RIG
DGE BSHES SMON LAM BZANG PO RIN CHEN

GYI DRUNG NAS DGE BSNYEN BSGRUBS, MING BLO BZANG BSTAN PA'I
RGYAL MTSAN ZHES GNANG, ZLA BA BRGYAD PA'I TSES

BCO LNGA LA RGYUD PA MKHAN PO NYA KY'A ZHABS DRUNG SOGS KYIS
GDAN SAR BKOD PA'I RTEN 'BREL BYAS, DGE BSHES

BLO BZANG CHOS 'BYOR DANG, KHU BO BLO BZANG PHUN TSOGS GNYIS
KLOG GI SLOB DPON DU BSTEN NAS, SBYOR SDEB

BLO 'DZIN GYI MGO TSUGS, DGUNG LO BDUN PA RAB BYUNG BCO LNGA
PA'I ME YOS LO'I ZLA BA LNGA PA'I TSES BZHI LA,

AA KY'A RIN PO CHE'I GSUNG BKOD LTAR SER SKYA'I DMAG BRGYA PHRAG
LHAG GI BSU MA DANG BCAS, RDO DKAR LAM

GSAR BRGYUD DE RANG SGAR AE WAm DGA' 'KHYIL DU PHEBS, DGE 'DUN
RNAMS KYIS SER SBRENG RGYA CHEN POS BSUS,

ZLA BA DRUG PA'I TSES BZHI LA DKA' CHEN BYANG CHUB RIN CHEN MDUN
NAS RAB BYUNG BSGRUBS SHING, MING BLO BZANG

BYANG CHUB BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME BTAGS, SKU GONG MA'I MCHOD DPON
SNGAGS RAMS PA KHRE TZI BSTAN PA DAR RGYAS SLOB

DPON DU BSTEN NAS DPE 'DZIN GANG MKHO LEGS PAR SBYANGS, DGUNG LO
BRGYAD PA SA 'BRUG LO'I ZLA BA BZHI PA'I

TSES NYER LNGA LA GDAN SAR HOR DMAG 'DZUL NAS NYAMS CHAG BYUNG
BAR BRTEN, GSOL CAN TZAM YANG KHYER LONG

MA BYUNG BAR 'DU KHANG CHEN MO'I STENG DU BROS TE, RJE GSUNG
'BYON MA'I SKU BRNYAN GYI G-YAS SU KHANG MIG GSUM

PAR NYIN ZHAG BDUN TZAM GAB NAS BZHUGS DGOS THUG ZLA BA LNGA
PA'I TSES GNYIS KYI NUB MOR GNYER PA 'JAM

DBYANGS RGYAL MTSAN DANG, LAS SNE BLO LDAN 'GA'I BLO THABS LA
BRTEN NAS GSANG STABS KYIS RDO DKAR LAM

GSAR DANG, LCANG RAR ZHANG PO TSANG BRGYUD DE RANG YUL DU PHEBS,
LO GCIG TZAM RING, BSAM GLING DANG,

DHI TSA DGON SOGS SU BYON, MDO SNGAGS KYI GZHUNG 'GA' BLOR 'DZIN
MDZAD, DGUNG LO DGU PA SA SBRUL LO'I

ZLA BA DRUG PA'I TSES NYER GCIG LA AA BA GHA WANG DANG, CHOS RJE
'JAM DBYANGS CHOS 'PHEL GYIS GDAN 'DREN

YI GE 'BYOR BAR BRTEN, DMAG MANG PO'I SKYEL GROGS DANG BCAS GDAN
SAR PHEBS, ZLA BA BDUN PA'I TSES

BCU LA DKA' CHEN BYANG CHUB RIN CHEN MDUN NAS YON TAN GZHIR GYUR
MA SOGS LUNG DU MA GSAN, GDAN SAR

ZLA BA GCIG BZHUGS TE ZLA BA BDUN PA'I TSES NYER GCIG LA SGAR
NAS BTEGS, SOG PO'I YUL PHYOGS

SU CHIBS KHA BSGYUR, RGYA SOG MGO PA AER TZI LI NAS CHU BZANG
DGON BAR BSKYAL, SKYABS RJE CHU BZANG RIN

@61 

PO CHE MJAL, DE NAS GAN CHEN DANG, 'JU LAG BRGYUD, MCHOD
RTEN THANG DU 'BYOR, DER BKA' CHOS CI

RIGS ZHUS RJES RIM PAR PHEBS NAS BKA' 'GYUR TSANG GI BLA BRANG
DU ZHAG NYER GNYIS BAR SKU NGAL GSOS NAS

BZHUGS, DE NAS RIM BZHIN LAM DU ZHUGS, LAM BAR RGYA SOG GI DMAG
MANG PO PHAR TSUR RGYU YANG, KHONG LA

SKYON MA BYUNG BAR MA ZAD, AA BA GHA WANG SOGS KYIS BSU MA RIM
PA DU MAR MNGAGS PA RNAMS 'BYOR TE, RTA

DANG, GZIMS GUR, KHYOGS SOGS CI DGOS TSANG MA 'BYOR, ZLA BA BCU
GCIG PA'I TSES BCU GNYIS LA SKU

GONG MA'I BLA BRANG DANG NYIN LAM GCIG 'GYANGS PA'I BAR AA BA
GHA WANG RANG NYID RTA PA GNYIS BRGYA LHAG DANG

BCAS BSU BAR 'BYOR, MCHOD YON RNAM GNYIS ZHAL THOG MAR MJAL,
PHYI NYIN BLA BRANG NOR 'DZIN DGA' TSAL

DU PHYAG PHEBS, AA BA GHA WANG GI MNGA' 'OG HO SHO'I BLA DPON
CHE CHUNG TSANG MAS MAndL RTEN GSUM DANG DNGOS

ZONG RGYA CHE PHUL ZHING, DKAR SPRO DMAR SPRO SOGS GSOL STON
GZABS RGYAS BSTABS, DGUNG LO BCU GCIG PA

LCAGS LUG LOR, THU'U BKVAN RIN PO CHE MJAL BA'I DON DU CHA HAR
PHEBS, THU'U BKVAN NAS ZAB CHOS 'GA'

GNANG, DE GA'I DGON PA YONGS SU PHEBS SHING YO BYAD 'BOR CHEN
DANG DGON GZHIS KA DANG BCAS PA 'BUL

MKHAN YANG BYUNG, LO DE'I ZLA BA BCU GCIG PAR RGYA NAG RI BO
RTZE LNGAR PHEBS, LO GCIG TZAM BZHUGS, CHU 

SPREL LO'I ZLA BA DGU PA'I TSES NYER GCIG LA DBUS SU PHEBS PA'I

MTHA' CHOS, SLOB GNYER GYI MGO BTZUGS TE,

SNYAN NGAG SOGS RIG NGAS CHE CHUNG TSANG MA LA SLOB GNYER
MDZAD, LO LNGA TZAM SLOB GNYER MDZAD RJES GZTANG

NGAM RING DU BYON NAS ZLA BA DRUG TZAM 'GOR, DE NAS RANG YUL
PHU PHAG DGOS DU TSUR LOG  DRUNG PA COS RJE'I

MDUN SNGAR MA THOB PA'I ZAB CHOS MANG PO ZHUS, DGUNG LO BCO
BRGYAD PA SHING SPREL LO'I ZAL BA BZHI PA'I TSES

BCO LNGA'I NYIN GUNG LA, NGOR CHEN GYIS MKHAN PO DANG DRUNG PA
CHOS RJES GSANG STON MDZAD NAS BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI

SDOM PA YANG DAG PAR MNOS, BSRUNG BYA MTHA' DAG TSUL BZHIN
BSRUNGS, NYIN DER KHONG DRUNG PA CHOS RJE'I

GDAN KHRIR MNGA' GSOL BAR MDZAD CING, DRUNG PA RANG NYID KYI
NA BZA' DANG PHYAG DRIL SOGS BLA CHAS TSANG

BAR GNANG, DGUNG LO NYI SHUR PHEBS PA ME PHO KHYI'I LOR SA GA
ZLA BA'I TSES BDUN PA'I NYIN GUNG LA DRUNG PA

CHOS RJE ZHI BA'I DBYINGS SU THIM, DE NAS MI RING BAR YAB
'DAS, KHONG THUGS SKYO BA GNYIS BRTZEGS KYIS

MNAR, 'DUS BYAS KYI CHOS LA YID BRTAN MED PAR DGONGS NAS, DBEN
PAR BYA BRAL DU BZHUGS, LO DE'I

DBYAR GNAS LA PHEBS 'DOD MED KYANG, MKHAN POS NAN TAN GYIS
BSKUL BAR BRTEN, DBYAR GNAS SU TSAD

MA RIGS GTER SOGS KYI BSHAD PA MDZAD, DGUNG LO NYER GNYIS PAR,
PAn CHEN BYAMS PA GLING PA BDE BAR

GSHEGS, LO GSUM RING PAn CHEN BYAMS GLING PA'I GDAN SAR
BZHUGS, DPE GZIGS DANG GZHUN GBSHAD RGYA

CHEN MDZAD, BLA MA KHAMS STON PA DANG MNYAM DU, STOD GANGS RI
MTSO GSUM BSKOR BA DANG, GNAS CHEN CHU

MIG BRGYA RTZAR MJAL SKOR DU PHEBS, DER RGYA GAR DZO KI PA'I
RNAL 'BYOR PA RNAMS LA DZO KI SKAD THOG NAS DAM  

CHOS BSHAD, DZO KI MKHAS PLA RNAMS KYIS BSNGAGS PAR MDZAD,
DGUNG LO NYER BDUN PAR DBUS SU CHOS MJAL

DU PHEBS NAS ZLA BA DRUG TZAM 'GOR, LO DE'I DGUN KHAR YANG
DBUS LHA LDAN DU PHEBS, MTSUR PHUR BKA'

BRGYUD CHOS SKOR RDZOGS PAR ZHUGS, DE NAS LHO MON DU BYON NAS
'GRO DON YUN RING MDZAD, DGUNG LO SO

GCIG PA ME MO BYA LOR (1537) ZLA BA GSUM PA'I TSES BDUN GYI
MTSAN PHYED LA DRIN CAN GYI YUM DGUNG GRANGS

NGA GSUM LAS MA LON PA DE NYID 'DAS, MA DRIN CHEN DANG BRAL
BA'I SDUG BSNGAL GYIS MNAR, DGE RDZOGS RGYA

CHEN BSGRUBS, GSER MDOG CAN DANG, STAG LUNG SOGS SU SKU GSUNG
THUGS KYI RTEN GSAR BZHENGS DANG,

'JAM DBYANGS MKHYEN BRTZE DBANG PO MCHOG NI, YAB GNYOS KYI RIGS
LAS DPAL 'BRI GUNG BYANG CHUB

GLING PA'I DBON BRGYUD SDE DGE'I DRUNG CHEN RIN CHEN RNAM RGYAL
DANG, YUM SOG BZA' DGE RAB GNYER CHEN

MGON TSE'I BU MO BSOD NAMS MTSO GNYIS KYI SRAS SU RAB BYUNG BCU
BZHI PA'I LCAGS 'BRUG LO'I (1820) HOR

ZLA DRUG PA'I TSES LNGA LA, MDO KHAMS SDE DGE GTER KLUNG DIL
MGO'I GRONG GI DBYAR RU KHYUNG CHEN BRAG GI NYE

'DABS SU SKU 'KHRUNGS,

DGUNG LO BZHI LNGA TZAM NAS YI GE'I LJAGS KLOG GSAN, SKU CHUNG
NGU'I DUS NAS MKHYEN RAB KYI RTZAL

RDZOGS PAS 'BRI KLOG SOGS TSEGS MED DU MKHYEN, DGUNG LO BCU
GNYIS THOG THAR RTZE MKHAN CHEN BYAMS PA

KUN DGA' BSTAN 'DZIN GYIS, AE WAm THAR PA RTZE'I MKHAN CHEN
BYAMS PA NAM MKHA' 'CHI MED KYI YANG SRID DU

NGOS BZUNG, 'JAM DBYANGS MKHYEN BRTZE DBANG PO KUN DGA' BSTAN
PA'I RGYAL MTSAN DPAL BZANG PO ZHES

MTSAN GSOL, DGUNG LO NYER GCIG PAR SMIN GLING MKHAN CHEN RIG
'DZIN BZANG PO LAS BSNYEN PAR RDZOGS,

DBUS SE 'BRAS DGE GSUM DANG, GTZANG SA NGOR SOGS GDAN SA CHEN PO
RNAMS SU BYON, SMIN GLING KHRI CHEN

'GYUR MED SANGS RGYAS KUN DGA' DANG, ZHE CHEN 'GYUR MED MTHU
STOBS RNAM RGYAL, SA SKYA PA RDO RJE RIN CHEN,

THAR RTZE MKHAN CHEN SKU MCHED SOGS SA DGE BKA' RNYING GI BLA MA
SKYES BU DAM PA BRGYA DANG LNGA BCU LHAG YONGS

'DZIN DU BSTEN, BZO GSO SGRA TSAD YAN LAG DANG BCAS PA THUN MONG
RIG PA'I GNAS RNAMS DANG, DBU PHAR

'DUL MDZOD SOGS RGYU MTSAN NYID THEG PA'I GZHUNG BSHAD SKOR, BDE
DGYES GSANG GSUM, DUS 'KHOR GSANG

SNYING SOGS 'BRAS BU GSANG SNGAGS RDO RJE THEG PA'I RGYUD SDE'I
ZAB KHRID BCAS MDO SNGAGS RIG GNAS DANG

BCAS PA'I GZHUNG MTHA' DAG LA THOS BSAM GYIS SGRO 'DOGS BCAD,
GANGS CAN GYI LJONGS SU MAN NGAG SNGON GYI

PHYAG SROL MA NYAMS PAR YOD PA THAMS CAD SO SO'I KHUNGS DANG
'BREL BA'I YONGS 'DZIN GTZUG TU BSTEN TE

SMIN BYED KYI DBANG DANG, GROL BYED KYI KHRID, RGYAB RTEN GYI
LUNG DANG BCAS PA TSANG MA MA NOR BA ZHAL NAS SNYAN

DU BRGYUD DE THUGS KYI DPAL BER GTAMS, RGYAL BA'I BKA' 'GYUR RIN
PO CHE DANG, RNYING MA RGYUD 'BUM,

BSTAN 'GYUR GYI KHROD LAS LUNG RGYUN GANG BZHUGS SO COG GI GTZOS
'PHAGS BOD RIS MED KYI GSUNG CHOS YONGS

BSDOMS GLEGS BAM BDUN BRGYA TZAM GYI BKLAG LUNG RNAMS SKU NGAL
KHYAD DU BSAD DE 'BAD BRTZON CHEN POS

GSAN BZHES MDZAD CING, SGOM SGRUB NYAMS LEN MDZAD PAS NYAMS
RTOGS KHYAD PAR CAN THUGS LA 'KHRUNGS,

RJE 'DI NYID KYIS MDO RGYUD MAN NGAG DANG BCAS PA GANG GSAN PA
THAMS CAD GDUL BYA SO SO'I MOS

SKAL DANG 'TSAM PAR DBANG LUNG KHRID GSUM GYI RGYUN BSKYANGS PAS
PHYOGS DANG RIS SU MA CHAD PA'I RGYAL BA'I

BSTAN PA YONGS RDZOGS GZHIR BZHENGS SU BSLANGS, SKYE 'GRO RNAMS
SMIN CING GROL BA'I LAM LA BKOD, RJE'I

CHEN RNAMS DANG, SA SKYA'I KHRI CHEN BKRA SHIS RIN CHEN, NA

PAR DU BKOD PA PO TI BZHI BCU LA NYE BA DANG,

STENG GI MCHOD SDONG CHEN MO GTZOS BRGYA LHAG

TZAM GSER ZANGS KYIS BSKRUN, SKU GSUNG THUGS KYI RTEN DE DAG
BZHUGS SU GSOL BA'I LHA KHANG CHE CHUNG BCU

SMAD KYI CHAR GTOGS PA KHRA DING ZHES PA'I YUL

YIN, RAB BYUNG BCU GCIG PA'I SA PHO BYI BA'I LO'I (1648) HOR ZLA
DANG PO'I TSE BRGYAD LA, YAB DPAL

'BUM RGYAL DANG YUM THAR MO BYAMS GNYIS KYI SRAS SU 'KHRUNGS,
DGUNG LO BDUN PAR YAB KYI GCEN PO DGE

SLONG BSOD NAMS LHUN GRUB MDUN 'BRI KLOG DANG LHA RIS BCAS
SBYONG, DGUNG LO BCU GSUM PAR KHYU MCHOG YE

SHES RGYA MTSO'I SPYAN SNGAR DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA BLANGS, MTSAN
BLO BZANG RGYAL MTSAN GSOL, DGUNG LO BCU DRUG

NAS NYI SHU'I BAR, SKU CHINGS MI BKROL BAR GZIMS PA SOGS DKA'
SPYAD DANG DGE SBYOR MDZAD CING, SNGAGS

KYI BKLAG THABS DANG, SMAN DPYAD, RTZIS SOGS SBYANGS, DGUNG LO
NYER GCIG PAR DBUS SU PHEBS,

'BRAS SPUNGS SGO MANG GRVA TSANG DU SLOB GNYER MDZAD, DGUNG LO
NYER DRUG PAR GSANG PHUR SA DGE'I GRVA TSANG BCU

GCIG TSOGS PA'I DBUS SU DAM BCA' BZHAG  MKHAS PA'I GRAGS PA DBUS
GTZANG YONGS SU KHYAB, DGUNG LO

NYER BDUN PAR LNGA PA CHEN PO'I MDUN NAS DGE SLONG GI SDOM PA
MNOS, 'JAM MGON BLO GROS RGYA MTSO, LCANG

SKYA NGAG DBANG CHOS LDAN, BKA' 'GYUR SBYIN PA RGYA MTSO, RGYAL
SRAS MER RGAN SOGS BLA MA MANG DU BSTEN,

DGUNG LO SO GNYIS PAR RI BO DGE 'PHEL DU PHEBS, LO NYI SHU'I
RING SNGAGS KYI SKOR GSAN SBYONG MDZAD,

DGUNG LO NGA GSUM PAR T'A LA'I TSANGS DBYANGS RGYA MTSOS SGO
MANG GI BLA MA BSKOS NAS GDAN KHRIR PHEBS,

SKABS DER GZHUNG POD LNGA'I 'CHAD NYAN DANG GSUNG CHOS RTZOM PA
KHO NAS DUS 'DA' BAR MDZAD, DGUNG LO DRUG

CU PAR LHA BZANG KHANG NAS PHA BONG KHA'I GDAN SA PHUL NAS KHRIR
PHEBS, LO GSUM TZAM BZHUGS, DGUNG LO RE

'JU MI PHAM RGYA MTSO NI YAB MGON PO DAR RGYAS DANG, YUM SRING
CHUNG GNYIS KYI SRAS SU, RAB BYUNG

BCU BZHI PA'I ME PHO RTA'I LO (1846) LA SDE DGER ZLA CHU'I NYER
'GRAM YA CHU DING CHUNG ZHES PAR 'KHRUNGS,

DGUNG LO DRUG PA NAS YAB DANG ZHANG PO SOGS KYI MDUN 'BRI KLOG
DANG, RTZIS DKAR NAG GI SNGON 'GRO BCAS

SBYANGS, DGUNG LO BCU PA NAS 'BRI KLOG THOGS MED DU GYUR CING
GSUNG RTZOM THUNG NGU'ANG CI RIGS MDZAD,

DGUNG LO BCU GNYIS PAR SNYING DGON GSANG SNGAGS CHOS GLING DU
GRVA BTZUN MDZAD, DGUNG LO BCO BRGYAD PAR

ZHANG PO DANG LHAN DU LHA LDAN DU PHEBS, DGA' LDAN DGON PAR ZLA
GCIG TZAM BZHUGS, DE NAS LHO BRAG MKHAR

CHU SOGS SU GNAS MJAL PHEBS RJES SDE DGER PHYIR PHEBS, KHONG GI
RTZA BA'I BLA MA 'JAM DBYANGS MKHYEN BRTZE

DBANG PO DANG GZHAN YANG DBANG CHEN DGYES RAB RDO RJE, DPAL
SPRUL 'JIGS MED CHOS DBANG SOGS MKHAS PA

MANG PO SLOB DPON DU BSTEN NAS RIG PA'I GNAS KUN LA SBYANGS PA
MTHAR PHYIN MDZAD, LHAG PAR BZO DANG

GSO BA RTZIS RIG SKOR MDZAD RJES SNGA NA MED PA BSKRUN, DBUS
GTZANG KHAMS GSUM GYI RIS MED MKHAS PA

YONGS KYIS BSTOD TSIG GI ME TOG PHYOGS BRGYAR GTOD, MKHAS PA'I
GRAGS PA RGYAL KHAB YONGS SU KHYAB, KHONG

GI BZHUGS GNAS GTZO BO, DKAR MO STAG TSANG DGON DANG, 'JU RI
KHROD, LDAN KHOG DING MGO RI KHROD

BCAS YIN, DGUNG GRANGS DRUG CU RE BDUN DU PHEBS PA, RAB BYUNG
BCO LNGA PA'I CHU BYI LO'I (1912) ZLA BA

002419 PAR MA,...

DAM PA'I CHOS RIN PO CHE 'PHAGS PA'I YUL DU JI LTAR DAR BA'I
TSUL GSAL BAR STON PA DGOS 'DOD KUN 'BYUNG ZHES BYA BA BZHUGS
SO, ,...(2) 131

RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS NYUNG BSDUS,...

RVA YI RUS BRGYUD DU GRAGS PA'I RJE BTZUN T'A RA NA THA NI
DBUS DANG GTZANG GNYIS KYI MTSAMS DBUS

KYI KHONGS SU JO MO KHA RAG DANG NYE BA'I SAR, CHOS RJE KUN
DGA' SENG GES BTAB PA'I CHOS 'KHOR SDINGS KYI

DGON GNAS, 'BRANG ZHES PA'I YUL DU, YAB RNAM RGYAL PHUN TSOGS
DGUNG LO ZHE DRUG PA DANG, YUM RDO RJE BU

DGA' BGRANG BYA BCU DGU PA GNYIS KYI SRAS SU, RAB BYUNG BCU
PA'I SHING MO PHAG GI LO'I (1575) ZLA BA DRUG  

PA'I TSES BRGYAD KYI NYI MA RTZE SHAR LA SKU BLTAMS SO,
,BLTAMS MA THAG PA'I DUS SU GROD BUS G-YOGS PA'I

RNAM PA CAN DU YOD PAS, MES POS LDE MIG GIS GROD BU'I RGYA
DRAL BA SOGS KYI RTEN 'BREL MDZAD, SKABS

DER KHYE'U SKRA DKAR PO YENG YENG BA ZHIG YOD PAS, MES POS
KHYE'U SKRA DKAR PO 'DI'I RIGS LA SHES RAB

@190

CHEN PO YONG BAS, GRIB KYIS MA BSGRIBS PAR GYIS GSUNGS, MING
SRI GCOD RDO RJE BTAGS, DGUNG LO

GNYIS PA TZAM LA, 'KHRU NAD DRAG POS BTAB, SNA'ANG ZHOM, PHAL
CHER 'CHI BAR NYE BA NA, AA KHUS SMAN

BCOS MDZAD DE RIM GYIS DVANGS, 'ON KYANG LO 'GA'I BAR SMRA BA
NYUNG BAS KUN GYIS LKUGS PA ZHIG YONG NGAM

SNYAM PA BYUNG, DGUNG LO BZHI PAR PHEBS PA NA, SMRA SHES PAR
GYUR CING RGYUN DU NGA BLA MA KUN DGA' GROL

MCHOG YIN, NYE GNAS DPAL 'BYOR ZER BA ZHIG YOD ZER BA BYUNG,
BYIS PA'I BLA RDOL GYI GTAM DE, YAR

'BROG KHRI DPON BSTAN 'DZIN DBANG RGYAL SOGS, KUN DGA' GROL
MCHOG GI YON BDAG BU CHEN RNAMS KYI

SNYAN LAM DU SONG, DE DAG GIS BSKUL MA'I 'OG JO NANG MKHAN PO
LUNG RIGS RGYA MTSOS, JO NANG BLA MA KUN

DGA' GROL MCHOG GI SKYE PHRENG DU NGOS 'DZIN MDZAD, LO DE'I
ZLA BA DGU PA'I TSES NYER LNGAR BTEG STE JO

DGON PHYOGS SU BYON, YAB YUM GYIS BKRA SHIS BRAG GI BAR SKYEL
MA MDZAD DE, YUN RING BAR BYIS PA'I RJES

SU BLTAS, RIM BGROD KYIS RGYAL RTZER SLEBS, DER ZLA PHYED
BZHUGS RING MKHAS GRUB SANGS RGYAS YE SHES  

MJAL ZHING, THUGS DGYES PA CHEN POS DUS 'KHOR GYI DBANG ZHIG
KYANG BSTZAL, DE NAS RIM BZHIN GSER

MDOG CAN DU PHEBS, ZHAG LNGA TZAM NAS BTEG  RI KHROD CHEN PO JO
MO NANG DU 'BYOR, PHEBS LAM DU ZLA BA

GNYIS TZAM 'GOR, MI RING BAR CHO 'PHRUL DUS CHEN TSUGS, GROL
RJES RDO RINGS PA CHEN PO 'JAM DBYANGS

KUN DGA' RGYAL MTSAN DRUNG DU SGROL DKAR GYI RJES GNANG THOG
MA'I RTEN 'BREL DU ZHUS, DE MIN GYI DBANG DANG

RJES GNANG SOGS MANG DU ZHUS, GZHAN YANG RJE BTZUN BRAG STOD
PA DANG, JO NANG RJE DRUNG RIN PO CHE BCAS

LA'ANG LUNG RJES GNANG 'GA' ZHIG ZHUS, YAR LAM YON BDAG RNAMS
KYIS PHUL BA'I DNGOS RDZAS SUM CHA TZAM

SMON 'GRO BAR PHUL ZHING YON MCHOD 'BREL ZAB BYAS, 'ON KYANG
BRJOD GLENG SNA TSOGS LA BRTEN NAS, SMON

'GRO BA SKU MCHED DANG 'BREL BA LEGS PO RANG MA BYUNG, DGUNG
LO DRUG PA LCAGS PHO 'BRUG LO'I ZLA BA DANG

PO'I TSES GCIG LA KLOG SLOB PA'I DBU BTZUGS, SBYOR KLOG LO
GCIG LHAG LA MTHAR PHYIN, DE NAS BLOR

'DZIN GYI DBU TSUGS, GTING SKYES CHOS GRVAR LO PHYED TZAM
BZHUGS, DE NAS STAG LUNG RDZONG BRGYUD CHOS SDE BLA

BRANG DKAR POR LO PHYED LHAG BZHUGS, SKABS DE'I LO GCIG LHAG
LA CHOS SPYOD RNAMS BLO LA CHUD CING,

DBANG RJES GNANG SOGS CHOS BKA' DPAG TU MED PA THOB, DGUNG LO
BRGYAD PA CHU PHO RTA LO'I ZLA BA DANG

PO'I TSES NYER LNGAR JO DGON CHOS LUNG DU PHEBS, GSER MDOG CAN
GYI MKHAN SLOB RNAMS DANG, JO NANG

PA'I SGRUB PA MO KUN KHONG MJAL BAR YONG, CHO 'PHRUL DUS CHEN
SKABS SU TSOGS LA PHEBS, MKHAN RIN

PO CHE'I ZHABS DRUNG DANG, BLA MA 'JAM DBYANGS SOGS KYIS,
MKHAS DBANG BYAMS PA LHUN GRUB NYID NI MKHAS

BTZUN GYI YON TAN DANG LDAN ZHING, RJE GONG MA'I DNGOS SLOB
DRI MA MED PA YIN PAS, KHYED KYI SLOB DPON DU

BSTEN 'OS ZHES SLOB DPON DU BSKOS, ZLA BA GNYIS PA'I TSES GCIG
NYIN SLOB DPON GYI MDUN DU, TSAD MA

RIGS GTER BLOR 'DZIN GYI MGO BRTZAMS, ZLA BA LNGA TZAM LA BLOR
CHUD, CHOS MDZAD KUN RGYAN PA SOGS BYANG

STAG LUNG DU, STAG LUNG PA KUN DGA' BKRA SHIS RGYAL MTSAN GDAN
'DREN DU MNGAGS, ZLA BA BDUN PA'I TSES 

@191

BCU BDUN NYIN STAG LUNG PA CHOS LUNG DU 'BYOR, KHONG GI MDUN NAS
BKA' GDAMS GLEGS BAM GYI LUNG ZHUS,

LO DE'I ZLA BA BRGYAD PA'I TSES LNGA NYIN PAR SNGA MOR CHOS LUNG
BYANG RTZE'I MCHOD KHANG GI YANG THOG TU PHEBS TE,

MA CHEN CHOS YE PAS DBU SKRA BREGS PA SOGS RAB BYUNG GI RTAGS
MIN PA RNAMS YONGS SU DOR NAS, SNGA DRO'I

CHU TSOD DGU PA TZAM LA RJE STAG LUNG PA CHEN PO'I SPYAN SNGAR

SGOS GANG RUNG ZHIG TU DKAR ME'I RGYUN GANG

'BYOR ZHIG DANG BCAS TE BYUNG NA BSAM PA YIN PAS 'DOD MOS LTAR
CIS KYANG DGOS'' ZHES ZHUS PAR DON MA

THOB, SENG GE RTZER ZHUS NAS DPAL SDINGS SAM GANGS CAN GANG RUNG
ZHIG DGOS ZHES ZHUS PA'ANG DGON KHAG

GZHAN GYIS CHAGS SDANG GIS BKAG STE MA BYUNG, DON DE JI LTAR
BYAS NAS 'ONG SNYAM DU DGONGS PA BTANG BAS

SNGAR RJE SHES RAB SENG GE BSAM GRUB RTZE NAS SNAR THANG LA BYON
RIM BZHIN BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I DGON SA 'DI

LA PHYAG MDZUB GTAD DE SA PHYOGS 'DI NA DGE 'DUN GRUB MGO BO
SKYA YER YER CHOS 'CHAD KYIN YOD PA ZHIG

RGYUN DU 'CHAR SNANG 'ONGS KYI 'DUG GSUNGS PA ZHIG YANG YANG YOD
PAR BRTEN SA PHYOGS DE GA RANG DU BZANG

BAR GZIGS TE DGON PA 'DEBS PA'I THUGS THAG BCAD, BSAM GRUB
RTZE'I BRAG DMAR BLA BRANG DU RTEN

BZHENGS KYI 'GO BTZUGS, THOG MA'I LUGS PHUD DU RJE BTZUN SGROL
MA'I SKU ZHIG DANG, STON PA'I SKU MTHO

NYER LNGA CAN LUGS MA GZI 'OD 'BAR BA GZUNGS BZHUGS KHYAD PAR
CAN GYIS BSGRUBS PA ZHIG BZHENGS,

SBYIN BDAG DAR RGYAS DPON BSOD NAMS DPAL BZANG GIS MDZAD NAS ME
MO YOS LO'I SMIN DRUG ZLA BA'I YAR

TSES BZANG POS RJE RANG NYID KYIS GTZOS SBYIN BDAG DANG BCAS PA
'DIR PHEBS TE GTZUG LAG KHANG DANG,

BLA BRANG, BRANG KHANG BCAS PA'I 'GRAM BTING STE BKRA SHIS LHUN
PO DPAL GYI SDE CHEN PO PHYOGS THAMS CAD

LAS RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I GLING DE BTAB, DE NAS LUNG NAG RDZONG
DANG, DPAL SDINGS, SNAR THANG SOGS LA RIM

BZHIN BYON, 'CHAD NYAN RGYUN MA CHAD PAR MDZAD, DPAL GSANG BA
'DUS PA'I DKYIL 'KHOR CHEN PO BZHENGS

TE NANG RTEN NGO MTSAR CAN DE LA RAB GNAS DANG MNGA' GSOL RGYAS
PAR MDZAD, DE NAS RNAM SRAS GLING DU

DBYAR GNAS MDZAD PA'I ZHABS TOG BSAM GRUB RTZE NAS BSGRUBS, DGAG
DBYE THOG NAS RJE DPON SLOB RNAMS

BKRA SHIS LHUN POR PHEBS TE DER GZHI PHAB STE BZHUGS PA'I THOG
MA DE NAS MDZAD, ME SBRUL LO'I DGUN CHOS

NAS 'GO BRTZAMS TE GRVA PA RNAMS KYIS KYANG BKRA SHIS LHUN POR
BZHUGS PA'I MTHIL MDZAD, SA PHO RTA LOR RJE

BLA MA 'DI RI BO DGE LDAN GYI MKHAN POR GDAN 'DREN PA BYUNG
YANG, BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I DGON PA 'DI

BTAB MA THAG TU SOG BAS RGYUN BRTAN PA ZHIG MA BYUNG KHA DANG,
RJE BTZUN TZONG KHA PA CHEN PO'I BSTAN PA

'BAB ZHIG LA DGONGS TE 'DI GAR SDOD PA YIN GSUNGS TE MI BYON PAR
THAG BCAD, SA SKYA PA CHOS RJE SENG

RGYAL GYI DRUNG NAS DMAR PO SKOR GSUM GYI MAN NGAG DANG, RTA
MGRIN YANG GSANG SOGS KYI RJES GNANG MAN

NGAG RNAMS ZHUS, RJE BTZUN SGROL MA'I GSER SKU MDA' TSAD MA SOGS
SKU MANG PO BZHENGS, DE NAS SHING PHO

SPRE'U'I LO LA PHYOGS KYI YIG MKHAN MANG PO BSDUS TE THUGS DAM
BKA' 'GYUR GYI GSUNG RAB DANG GOS SKU

@201

CHEN MO DKYUS SU 'DOM BCO BRGYAD DANG, ZHENG DU 'DOM BCU GNYIS
YOD PA MTSAR ZHING BYIN RLABS DANG

LDAN PA ZHIG BZHENGS TE GOS SKU 'DI'I THUGS KA NA RJE RANG NYID
KYIS MDZAD PA'I BSTAN PA RGYAS PA'I SMON LAM

GYI TSIG MANG PO ZHIG BRIS PAR MDZAD, DE NAS SKU GSUNG THUGS
RTEN GYI RTEN KHYAD PAR CAN MANG PO BZHENGS

PA 'DI RNAMS LA RJE RANG NYID KYIS RAB GNAS KYANG MDZAD, LHA SA
DANG, RI BO CHE, DGE LDAN, SNAR

THANG, KHRO PHU, GNAS RNYING, BO DONG SOGS KYI DGON SDE KHAG LA
MCHOD RDZAS GRANGS MED PAR PHUL ZHING, CHU

MO SBRUL LO'I DGUN CHOS GNYIS LA GRVA PA CHIG STONG DRUG BRGYA
TZAM LA GSOL PHOGS DANG, GSOL THUG SOGS KYI

ZHABS TOG LEGS PAR BSGRUBS TE CHOS 'KHOR RGYA CHEN PO BSKOR,
SHING PHO RTA LO'I CHO 'PHRUL CHEN PO'I ZLA BA

LA GNAS RNYING RIN PO CHES THOG DRANGS PHYOGS KYI BU SLOB KYI
BSTAN 'DZIN CHEN PO RNAMS KYANG SPYAN DRANGS NAS

TSOGS PA CHIG STONG DRUG BRGYA TZAM GYI SMON LAM BTZUGS, RJE
'DI'I SKU TSE 'DI LA 'DUL BA'I BSLAB KHRIMS

RNAM PAR DAG PA GZHIR BZUNG, GZHI GSUM GYI PHYAG LEN MA NYAMS
PA'I NGANG NAS BSHAD NYAN, RTEN BZHENGS,

GTZUG LAG KHANG BZHENGS PA, DKON COG GI MCHOD PA, GSUNG RAB KYI
RTZOM SOGS RGYUN MI CHAD PA'I MDZAD PA

NI SNGON CHAD GANGS RI'I KHROD 'DIR GZHAN GYIS SGRUN PAR DKA'
BA'I SNYAN PA'I GRAGS PA MTHA' YAS PAR

GYUR, SHING PHO RTA LOR STON MYANG STOD CHAB TSAN DU PHEBS TE,
PHU MDA'I SKYE BO'I TSOGS MTHA' YAS PA DAG

DANG, CHOS SDE CHE CHUNG NA BZHUGS PA'I DGE 'DUN RNAMS LA CHOS
DANG BYIN RLABS KYI BSNYEN BKUR SOGS

BDAG GIR MDZAD DE SNAR THANG BRGYUD SLAR YANG BKRA SHIS LHUN POR
PHEBS, LO 'DI'I ZLA BCU GCIG PA'I

TSES BDUN TZAM LA, ZHAL SKYUG CUNG ZAD 'ONG BA'I SKU KHAMS MA
BDE BA TZAM YOD LA, SNYUN ZUG CHEN PO

MED PAR CUNG ZAD THUGS NYOB PA'I RNAM PA BSTAN NAS SEMS DPA'
CHEN POS THOG DRANGS SLOB DPON GZHIS

BZHUGS RNAMS DRUNG DU BOS PAR MDZAD, RJE'I ZHAL NAS, KHYED RNAMS
KYIS SPYIR SANGS RGYAS KYI BSTAN PA

DANG, SEMS CAN GYI BDE SKYID, KHYAD PAR BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I
BSTAN PA LA BSAMS NAS JI SRID BAR DU

'DIR BZHUGS NAS BSHAD SGRUB TSUL BZHIN MDZAD NA NGED KYI BSAM PA
YANG DE GAS 'GRUB PA YIN ZHES ZAB

DANG RGYA CHE'I CHOS BKA' MANG PO BSTZAL NAS DE'I MTSAN MO THUGS
DAM LA RTZE GCIG TU MNYAM PAR BZHUGS TE

RAB BYUNG BRGYAD PA'I SHING RTA LO (1474) LA ZHI BAR GSHEGS SO,
,

GSUNG RAB NI DAM CHOS 'DUL BA'I GLENG 'BUM CHEN MO, MDO RTZA
DANG, SO THAR, RNAM 'GREL

BCAS KYI t'I KA CHAB SHOG SHAR GANGS RI MA SOGS NYAMS MGUR GYIS
MTSON GSUNG 'BUM POD LNGA YOD PA CHA

RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS NYUNG BSDUS,...

T'A LA'I SKU PHRENG GNYIS PA RJE DGE 'DUN RGYA MTSO NI GTZANG
RTA NAG TU YAB KUN DGA' RGYAL MTSAN

DANG, YUM KUN DGA' BZANG MO GNYIS KYI SRAS SU RAB BYUNG BRGYAD
PA'I ME SPRE LOR (1476) SKU BLTAMS,

DGUNG LO BCU GCIG TU PHEBS SKABS BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I GDAN SAR
KHRI 'DON THOG MDZAD SGO LEGS PAR

BSKYANGS, ME RTA LOR PAn CHEN LUNG RIGS RGYA MTSO'I MDUN NAS DGE
BSNYEN GYI SDOM PA BZHES, MTSAN DGE

'DUN RGYA MTSO ZHES GSOL, LO DE RANG GI DGUN CHOS SKABS GNAS
RNYING KUN DGA' BDE LEGS PAS MKHAN

PO DANG, PAn CHEN LUNG RIGS RGYA MTSOS SLOB DPON MDZAD DE DGE
TSUL GYI BSLAB PA BZHES SHING, GNAS

RNYING PA'I LUGS KYI MGON PO 'KHOR BRGYAD KYI RJES GNANG SOGS
CHOS BKA' 'GA' ZHIG GSAN, TSAD MA RNAM

'GREL GYI GZHUNG GSAN SBYONG MDZAD, DE RJES PAn CHEN YE SHES
RTZE MO BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I GDAN SAR PHEBS

PA YONGS 'DZIN DU BSTEN NAS MDO SNGAGS KYI DBANG LUNG MANG PO
GSAN, DGUNG LO BCU DRUG TZAM LA SNYAN

NGAG GI GZHUNG LA SLOB GNYER LEGS PAR MDZAD DE BLO GROS KYI
SNANG BA THOGS PA MED PAR RGYAS NAS RJE TZONG KHA

PA SOGS LA SNYAN NGAG GI TSIG RGYAN LA BRTEN NAS BSTOD PA ZHIG
BRTZAMS PA'I DBU TSUGS, DE NAS RGYAL RTZE

DPAL 'KHOR CHOS SDE SOGS LA PHEBS, DE SKABS SNAR THANG GI MKHAN
PO RGYAL BA GRAGS PAS DGE 'DUN RGYA

MTSO'I YAB LA HA CANG MI MNYES PA'I DBANG GIS ``MI ? 'DI'I BU LA
THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA'I SKU SKYE MI YONG ''ZER ?

BA SOGS KYIS BKRA SHIS LHUN POR BZHUGS BZOD MI BDE BA'I GNAS
TSUL BYUNG YOD KYANG, BZOD PA'I GO CHA

SNYING POR 'DZIN TE BZHUGS BZHIN PA'I SKABS 'BRAS SPUNGS PA'I
GDAN RABS BRGYAD PA 'JAM DBYANGS

LEGS PA CHOS 'BYOR SOGS KYIS DBUS PHYOGS SU SPYAN DRANGS, DGUNG
LO BCU DGU BZHES SKABS BKRA SHIS

LHUN PO NAS DBUS SU BTEGS TE DPAL LDAN 'BRAS SPUNGS SU PHEBS, LO
GSUM RING 'JAM DBYANGS LEGS

CHOS KYI DRUNG NAS PHAR TSAD DANG, 'DUL MDZOD, MNGON PA GONG 'OG
MDO SDE RGYAN SOGS NANG DON RIG PA'I

GZHUNG LUGS DU MA'I MDZUB KHRID DANG, RJE YAB SRAS KYI BKA' 'BUM
SOGS DBANG LUNG MANG PO ZHIG LEGS

PAR GSAN, DGUNG LO NYI SHU'I THOG GNAS RNYING KUN DGA' BDE LEGS
KYIS MKHAN PO DANG, 'JAM DBYANGS

LEGS CHOS KYIS LAS SLOB MDZAD DE BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI SDOM PA
BZHES, BYANG RA SGRENG DU BYON NAS RTEN RNAMS

MJAL, DE NAS LHO KHA BSAM YAS DANG, 'PHYONGS RGYAS, RTZED THANG
SOGS LA ZHABS KYIS BCAGS TE DAM

PA'I CHOS KYI SBYIN PA TSAD MED BSTZAL, DGUNG LO NYER LNGAR
PHEBS DUS NANG SO BRAG DKAR BA SRID CHOS RGYAL

@210

POS MTHUN RKYEN SBYAR TE BRAG YER PAR DRANG NGES RNAM 'BYED KYI
DKA' 'GREL DANG GRUB MTHA' SPYI'I RNAM BZHAG

CIG BKA' RTZOM MDZAD, LHO KHA KHUL RIN CHEN SGANG DU MKHAS GRUB
NOR BZANG RGYA MTSO'I MDUN NAS DUS

'KHOR RGYUD 'GREL GYI RTZIS CHA LAG YONGS RDZOGS DANG, DE NYID
KYIS MDZAD PA'I DUS 'KHOR SPYI DON GYI BSHAD

LUNG SOGS DBANG BKA' MANG PO GSAN, RJE DGE 'DUN RGYA MTSO RANG
NYID KYIS BRTZAMS PA'I DRANG NGES RNAM

'BYED KYI DKA' 'GREL SOGS BRTZAMS CHOS MANG PO SPYAN LAM DU PHAB
PAS THUGS KYI BUM BZANG GANG BAS

DGYES PA CHEN POR GYUR, SLAR YANG RA SGRENG DU THENGS GNYIS PA
PHEBS TE BKA' GDAMS PA'I GNAS RNAMS

MJAL, GNYAL SMAD NANG SO RIN CHEN DPAL BZANG GIS GDAN DRANGS PA
BZHIN GNYAL SDE DRUG GI DGON SDE'I

DGE 'DUN CHIG STONG TZAM 'DUS PA'I LUNG RA CHEN MO'I GRAL DBUR
PHEBS NAS CHOS BKA' ZAB RGYAS BSTZAL

BAS DGE 'DUN KUN YID 'PHROG PAR GYUR, NANG SO TSE DBANG PAS
MTHUN RKYEN SBYAR NAS TZ'A RI'I GNAS RNAMS

MJAL BAR PHEBS, LHO BRAG KHUL DANG, RTZED THANG, SHEL BRAG SOGS
LA BYON NAS SKYA SER MANG POR MDO

SNGAGS KYI CHOS BKA' DU MA BSTZAL TE RA SGRENG DU THENGS GSUM PA
PHEBS, RE ZHIG SKU MTSAMS SU BZHUGS TE

SGRUB PA NYAMS LEN MDZAD, DE NAS DVAGS PO KHUL DU ZHABS BCAGS TE
SGROM MDA' DGON GSAR LA DGA'

LDAN CHOS GLING ZHES MING 'DOGS PAR MDZAD, DGUNG LO SO BZHIR
PHEBS PA'I SA SBRUL LO (1509) LA RGYAL ME

TOG THANG DU DGON PA 'DEBS PA'I RE 'DUN BYUNG BA BZHIN GNAS DE
NYID DU ZHABS KYIS BCAGS TE SA

'DUL SOGS MDZAD, GTZUG LAG KHANG DNGOS GZHI DANG, GTZANG KHANG
SOGS KHYON KA CHEN BRGYAD CU THAM PA'I

RGYA KHYON GYI GRAM BTING, LO DE'I DBYAR KHAR 'DU KHANG GI THOG
YONGS RDZOGS PHUB THUB PA BYUNG STE DGON DER

GNAS BCA' ZHING, CHOS 'KHOR RGYAL LUNG RIGS SMRA BA SUM BRGYA'I
TSOGS RNAMS LA CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO BSKOR

BAR MDZAD PAS KUN DGA' BAS ROL BAR GYUR, DE NAS PAn CHEN YE SHES
RTZE MOS GZENGS BSTOD KYI ZHU YIG

DANG, BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I GDAN SAR CIS KYANG PHEBS DGOS PA'I ZHU
NAN BYUNG BAR BRTEN, SNGAR GYI GNAS

TSUL RNAMS THUGS SU MA BTAGS PAR BKRA SHIS LHUN POR BYON, GDAN
SA 'DZIN SKYONG GNANG DGOS LUGS YE

SHES RTZE MOS NAN GYIS GSOL RUNG RE ZHIG TZAM LAS RGYUN RING
BZHUGS RGYU'I THUGS MOS MED PAS GNAS SKABS

RING DGE 'DUN 'DUS TSOGS NYIS STONG SKOR LA TSAD MA'I GZHUNG
'CHAD NYAN DANG, BKA' GDAMS GLEGS BAM

SOGS KYI CHOS BKA' MANG DU BSTZAL NAS DGE 'DUN RNAMS KYI YID KYI
SHING RTA CHOS KYI NOR BUS GANG BAR

MDZAD DE SLAR YANG CHOS 'KHOR RGYAL DU PHEBS, DVAGS KONG KHUL
PHAL CHER DU PHEBS NAS CHOS SBYIN GYIS

BKANG BA MA ZAD, KONG PO RGYA MDA' KHUL DU YOD PA'I RI KHA BA
DANG, SANG SING DGON GNYIS PHAN TSUN MA

MTHUN PA'I 'GAL RKYEN BSAL NAS MTHUN SDEBS LUGS LEGS SU
BSKYANGS, SLAR BKRA SHIS LHUN POR PHEBS

TE GTZANG PHYOGS YUL GRU MANG POR CHOS SBYIN GYIS TSIMS PAR
MDZAD, ME GLANG LO (1517) LA PHAG GRU SDE SRID

NGAG DBANG BKRA SHIS GRAGS PA DANG, 'BRAS SPUNGS CHOS RJE LHA RI
PA, 'BRAS SPYI SO BCAS NAS GDAN SA

'BRAS SPUNGS KYI KHRI LA ZHABS SOR 'KHOD DGOS PA'I GSOL BA NAN
GYIS BTABS, LO 'DI'I ZLA BA BZHI PAR

@211

DPAL LDAN 'BRAS SPUNGS KYI GDAN KHRIR PHEBS SHING, 'CHAD RTZOD
RTZOM GSUM GYIS DUS 'DA' BAR MDZAD NAS

CHOS SDE 'DZIN SKYONG MDZAD, SNGA SOR LHA SA'I SMON LAM CHEN MO
LO NGO BRGYAD CU GYA GSUM TZAM GYI RING 'BRAS

SPUNGS KHO NAS 'DZIN SKYONGS THOG SER 'BRAS DGE GSUM GYI DGE
'DUN RNAMS 'DU TSOGS MDZAD BZHIN PA DE

LTAR YANG, SA RTA LOR (1498) SDE GZAR SKABS 'BRAS SPUNGS PA'I
SBYIN BDAG GTZO BO SNE'U RDZONG GI SDE SRID

LA YOR 'KHYOM BYUNG RKYEN LO NGO NYI SHU TZAM GYI RING LHA SA
NYE 'DABS KYI BKA' BRGYUD PA DANG, SA SKYA PA SOGS

KYI DGON SDE'I DGE 'DUN TSANG MA SMON LAM GYI TSOGS LA 'GRO BA
ZHIG BYUNG YOD, DE RJES PHAG GRU SDE SRID NGAG

DBANG BKRA SHIS GRAGS PA'I SRID DBANG NYAMS PA SLAR SOR CHUD
BYUNG BA DANG, LHAG PAR RJE DGE 'DUN RGYA

MTSO'I LUNG RIGS KYI YON TAN PHUL DU BYUNG BA'I SNYAN GRAGS DBUS
GTZANG, DVAGS KONG SOGS PHYOGS GANG

SAR KHYAB CHE BA'I DUS SKABS DANG 'PHEL BA BCAS KYIS BOD SA STAG
LO (1518) NAS BZUNG SLAR YANG 'BRAS

SPUNGS PAS SMON LAM CHEN MO'I 'DZIN SKYONG MDZAD, GDAN SA CHEN
PO GSUM GYI DGE 'DUN RNAMS SNGAR RGYUN

BZHIN TSOGS LA PHEBS, DE SKABS 'BRAS SPUNGS DGON PAR DGE 'DUN
CHIG STONG LNGA BRGYA SKOR DANG, SE

RAR DGE 'DUN SUM BRGYA TZAM LAS MED TSOD, LO 'DIR PHAG GRU SDE
SRID KYIS 'BRAS SPUNGS RDO KHANG SNGON PO

RJE DGE 'DUN RGYA MTSO'I BZHUGS GNAS SU SBYOR 'JAGS MDZAD, RTEN
'BREL CHED DU DGA' LDAN PHO BRANG ZHES

PA'I MING BTAGS, DUS MI RING BAR SE RA THEG CHEN GLING ZHOR
'DZIN MDZAD RJES GRVA TSOGS KYANG CHIG STONG

TZAM LA 'PHEL BA DANG, BSHAD SGRUB 'CHAD NYAN YANG DAR RGYAS SU
SONG, LCAGS GLANG LOR MNGA' RIS RGYAL PO

'JIG RTEN DBANG PHYUG PAD DKAR SDE DANG, BLON PO NGAG DBANG RNAM
RGYAL GNYIS KYIS RIN PO CHE'I 'BUL BA

SPAM MTHO BA DANG BCAS RAB BYUNG PA NGANG PA'I KHYU 'DRA BA MANG
PO BTANG BA LA GZHIR BYAS NAS BTZUGS PA'I

DGON SDE MNGA' RIS GRVA TSANG ZHES PA DE'I MING YANG DE NAS
THOGS PA YIN 'DUG DGUNG LO DRUG CU RE DRUG

TU PHEBS PA RAB BYUNG DGU PA'I LCAGS GLANG LOR (1541) 'BRAS
SPUNGS SU ZHI BA GSHEGS, DAD RTEN DNGUL

CHEN DANG, RNAM THAR SKOR, ZHAL

GNANG GIS BSDAMS RA MDZAD PA MA ZAD, SLOB GNYER SBYANGS 'BRAS
LEGS RIGS RNAMS LA GNANG CHA SOGS KYI

GZENGS BSTOD KYANG MDZAD, SHING BYI LOR GONG MA'I YAB KYI
BZHUGS GNAS RNYING PAR GTZUG LAG KHANG CHEN PO

``DGA' LDAN BYIN CHAGS GLING'' GSAR DU BSKRUN PAR TSO CHEN ZHE
DGU, KHAL KHA TSO BDUN, RGYA BOD KYI BTZUN

GSAR BLO RIG BZANG BA LNGA BRGYA BSDUS TE MDO SNGAGS DANG, RIG
GNAS, GSO RIG BCAS KYI GRVA TSANG BZHI

'DZUGS RGYUR BOD NAS BLA MA SLOB DPON RDZONG BDA' DGOS LUGS
PHEBS PA BZHIN MTSAN NYID GRVA TSANG GI BLA

MAR HAR GDONG RAB 'BYAMS PA NGAG DBANG CHOS 'PHEL, RGYUD PA
GRVA TSANG DU SRAD RGYUD BLA MA DKON MCHOG

BSTAN DAR, RIG GNAS GRVA TSANG DU RMO LCOG ZHABS DRUNG, GSO
RIG GRVA TSANG DU PHUN TSOGS 'DZAM GLING,

GDAN SA GSUM DANG RGYUD SOGS NAS DGE BSHES BCO BRGYAD RAM
'DEGS SU GTONG GNANG MDZAD PA RNAMS LA

GANG CI'I BKA' SLOB DANG SBRAGS RDZONG BDA' MDZAD, LCAGS RTA
LO, PHO LHA BSOD NAMS STOBS RGYAL GYI BU

WANG 'GYUR MED RNAM RGYAL GYI DON RKYEN SKOR BDE GZAR CHEN PO
BYUNG RJES LCAGS LUG LOR GONG MA'I SKU TSAB

'BYOR TE SNGAR PHAN BOD KYI DPON PO RNAMS NAS SRID KYI 'GAN
LEN BYAS KYANG, RDO RJE 'CHANG T'A LA'I BLA MA'I

ZHABS 'DEGS MI YONG BAR MA ZAD, CHAB SRID KYI LAR RGYA LA'ANG
MI 'TSAM PA DU MA BYUNG ZHING, BOD 'BANGS

SPYI LA PHAN PA BYUNG MI 'DUG PAS DA NAS CHOS SRID THAMS CAD
KYI 'GAN 'KHUR RJE BLA MA NYID NAS BZHES NA,

BSTAN PA DANG CHAB SRID LA PHAN PA SHIN TU CHE BAS NGES PAR
MDZAD DGOS, ZHABS ZHUR BKA' BLON BZHI BSKO

GZHAG BSKYANGS PA NI GUNG PAndI TA'I ROGS ZLAR DZA SAG MDO
MKHAR ZHABS DRUNG TSE RING DBANG RGYAL DANG, DZA

SAG THON PA SRI CHOD TSE BSTAN, RTZE MGRON DAR HAN NYI MA
RGYAL MTSAN BCAS BKA' BLON DU BSKO GZHAG

BSKYANGS THOG SE 'BRAS DGE GSUM GYI BLA MA LAS SNE DANG, BKA'
BLON MDA' DPON SOGS DRUNG 'KHOR RNAMS

BSDUS TE SLAD PHYIN LAS DON BYED PHYOGS SKOR GYI DON TSAN BCU
GSUM DRIL BSGRAGS DANG, BKA' SHAG GI THAM

KHA YIG 'BRUR SRID ZHI'I BDE SKYED ZHES PA GSAR BSGRUN MDZAD,
CHU BYA (1753) LOR SNGON DUS BOD DU LO PAn

MANG PO BYUNG BA'I SKABS RIG GNAS SO SO'I 'CHAD NYAN DAR RGYAS
CHE ZHING, T'A LA'I BLA MA SKU PHRENG LNGA PA'I DUS

PA'I SROL BZANG SHIN TU DAR NA'ANG, PHYIS

DGUNG LO SO BDUN PA SA MO SBRUL GYI LOR, RGYAL BA LNGA PA'I SKU
TSAB TU KHAL KHA AO ROD KYI 'KHRUG PA'I CHINGS 'GRIG LA PHEBS,
'KHRUG ZINGS 'JAGS RJES, GONG MAS PHO BRANG DU GDAN ZHUS MDZAD
DE, LCAGS RTA LO'I ZLA

BA BCU GNYIS PA'I TSES GSUM NYIN, GONG MA DANG MJAL 'PHRAD
MDZAD, MCHOD YON THUGS YID GCIG TU

'DRES SHING ZAB CHOS CI RIGS PHUL, GONG MAS BSTAN 'GRO'I DON DU
RGYA NAG TU BZHUGS DGOS PA'I BKA'

YANG YANG PHEBS, RE ZHIG NAS THABS MKHAS KYIS DGONGS PA ZHUS,
GONG MAS BLA MA'I BZHED PA LTAR BOD

PHYOGS SU GNAS SKABS PHEBS CHOG PA DANG, RING MIN SLAR YANG RGYA
NAG TU PHEBS DGOS PA'I BKA' GNANG

ZHING DNGUL GYI THAM KA DANG, CHO LO, GNANG SBYIN NGO MTSAR CAN
SOGS BDAG RKYEN BLA NA MED PA BSTZAL, RING

MIN PHO BRANG NAS BTEGS TE MTSO KHAR SBYIN BDAG RNAMS LA MJAL
'PHRAD DANG 'DON CHOS KYIS TSIM PAR

MDZAD, DE NAS KHAMS KYI GDAN SA RNAMS SU BYON NAS DAD LDAN RNAMS
LA CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO BSKOR TE RE ZHIG

BZHUGS, RING PO MA 'GYANGS PAR DBUS LHA LDAN DU CHIBS KHA THENGS
BZHI PA BSGYUR NAS, RGYAL DBANG LNGA PA

DANG, MTHON POR GNAS PA'I YON GYI BDAG PO RNAMS LA SKYES 'BUL
DANG MJAL PHYAG ZHUS PAR GZIGS SKYONG

DGYES TSOR TSAD MED BSTZAL, JO SH'AKA RNAM GNYIS SOGS RTEN RNAMS
LA MCHOD 'BUL DANG, SER 'BRAS

GSUM GYI DGE 'DUN GYI SDE RNAMS LA BSNYEN BKUR RLABS CHEN PO
SOGS RNAM DKAR GYI MDZAD 'PHRIN RGYA CHE'I

NGANG NAS RE ZHIG BZHUGS, SLAR YANG LNGA PA CHEN POR DGONGS PA
ZHUS NAS KHAMS KYI GDAN SA RNAMS SU

PHEBS, GDAN SA'I GRVA RIGS DANG YON BDAG TSANG MA CHOS DANG ZANG
ZING GIS TSIM PAR MDZAD, KHYAD PAR  DPA' SHOD DGA' LDAN RNAM
RGYAL PHO BRANG RTEN DANG BRTEN PAR BCAS PA 'GRAN PA'I ZLA THAMS
CAD DANG BRAL

BA DE NYID GSAR DU BSKRUN CING RAB GNAS DANG, DGA' STON GYI RIM
PA LEGS PAR MDZAD, KHONG GI SKU

RABS KYI PHRENG BA MA LUS PA PHO BRANG 'DI NYID DU ZHABS KYIS
BCAGS SHING, THOS BSAM SGOM GSUM GYI SGO

NAS RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA SPEL BA'I 'PHRIN LAS KYI 'OD STONG 'GYED
PA'I BSTI GNAS MCHOG TU GYUR, DE NAS

GONG MA CHEN PO'I BKA' BZHIN MA H'A TZI NA'I YUL DU CHIBS KYI
KHA LO THENGS GNYIS PA BSGYUR, RGYA NAG PE CING

DU GZUGS SKU'I BKOD PA CHOS DBYINGS SU THIM PA'I TSUL BSTAN,
GONG MA NAS DGONGS RDZOGS KYI CHOS SPRIN RGYA

CHER SPROS SHING, SLOB MA'I TSOGS KYIS KYANG DGONGS RDZOGS BYED
PA'I RNAM DKAR GYI DGE BA 'BYAMS KLAS PA

BSGRUBS, KHONG GI 'DAS LO DNGOS NI, KHONG GI SKYE 'PHRENG BLO
BZANG DPAL LDAN RGYAL MTSAN SA BYI LOR 'KHRUNGS

PAR DPAGS NA, KHONG DGUNG LO LNGA BCU NGA LNGAR PHEBS PA, RAB
BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I ME MO PHAG GI LOR 'DAS PA YIN NAM SNYAM PAR
DPYAD,

GSUNG NI, SNYAN NGAG DPER BRJOD DANG, BCA' YIG  'DON CHOG SKOR
BCAS BRIS MA POD GCIG NGED DPE MDZOD KHANG DU BZHUGS YOD, ,

BA SO SPRUL SKU SKU RABS BRGYAD PA RTA TSAG BSTAN PA'I MGON PO

PHO 'BRUG GI LOR (1760) SPO BO MAL JO ZHES PA'I GRONG DU
'KHRUNGS, DGUNG LO LNGA PA SHING SPREL LOR, RJE

DRUNG BLO BZANG DPAL LDAN RGYAL MTSAN GYI SKYE PHRENG DU NGOS
'DZIN BYAS TE SKU GONG MA'I GDAN SA DPA' SHOD

DGON DU GDAN DRANGS, DGUNG LO DRUG PA SHING BYA LOR KHRIR 'DON
MDZAD SGO ZAB RGYAS MDZAD CING, GONG MA

CHEN LUNG NAS THAM KA DANG 'JA' SA SNGAR BZHIN SOR GNAS CHOG
PA'I BKA' PHEBS, DGUNG LO BRGYAD PA ME

PHAG LOR, MKHAN CHEN DPAL LDAN SNYAN GRAGS PA'I DRUNG DU DGE
BSNYEN GYI SDOM PA ZHUS, DGUNG LO BCU

GNYIS PA LCAGS YOS LOR DPA' SHOD NAS SKU 'BUM DU GDAN DRANGS TE
DGUN GYI RING DER BZHUGS, DGUNG

LO BCU GSUM PA CHU 'BRUG LOR (1772) SKU 'BUM NAS SOG YUL DO LO
NOR BRGYUD ZHE HOR (KHRI TI) LA GONG

MA CHEN LUNG MJAL ZHING, GONG MAS RANG GI BYU RU'I PHYAG PHRENG
SOGS GNANG STE MTHONG BZO RGYA CHE BA MDZAD,

LCANG SKYA YE SHES BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME MDUN DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA
MNOS, YE SHES BLO BZANG BSTAN PA'I MGON

PO ZHES PA'I MTSAN GSOL, DE NAS SOG DO LO NOR DU LCAGS GLANG
LO'I BAR LO BCU RING DPAL LDAN GRAGS

PA YONGS 'DZIN DU BSTEN NAS 'DZIN SKYOR SOGS GSAN SBYONG LA
'BAD, GONG MA CHEN POS, GZIGS

BSKYANGS CHE BA'I NGANG NAS THAM KA BLA MA DANG 'DRA BAR DPON
G-YOG BCU GSUM GYI PHOGS LO LTAR BSTZAL,

LCANG SKYA YE SHES BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME SOGS KYI MDUN DBANG RJES
GNANG MANG DU ZHUS, DGUNG LO BCO LNGA PA

SHING RTA LOR YONGS 'DZIN DPAL LDAN GRAGS PA 'DAS, SHAR RTZE
MKHAN PO NO MIN HAN BLO BZANG 'JAM DPAL

YONGS 'DZIN DU BSTEN, BYANG CHUB LAM RIM GYI MYONG KHRID SOGS
DAM CHOS MANG DU GSAN, DGUNG LO NYER

GCIG PA LCAGS BYI LOR (1780) PAn CHEN DPAL LDAN YE SHES PE CING
DU PHEBS PA DANG LHAN CIG TU ZHE HOR

BKRA SHIS LHUN POR GONG MA MJAL 'PHRAD KYI MDZAD SGOR ZHUGS,
DGUNG LO NYER GNYIS PA LCAGS GLANG LOR DO

BYUNG BYAS NA LEGS TSUL SMRAS KYANG, YUM

'JUG SBYOR SDEB BLOR 'DZIN SOGS LA

PO'I RJES CHOG DANG CHOS 'DON SOGS GRONG

SKU BLO BZANG BSTAN 'DZIN DER PHEBS

MA'I RJES GNANG SOGS RJES GNANG SNA

CHOS 'BREL ZHUS, DGE 'PHEL RI KHROD

DU 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA'I RDO RJE'I MDUN ZLA BA GCIG LHAG TZAM
RING KHRID LUNG MANG PO ZHUS, DGUNG LO

NYER LNGA PA LCAGS 'BRUG LOR 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA'I RDO RJE SGO

NAS MI RING BAR SPYI KHANG GSAR SKRUN GYI LAS

GRVA BTZUGS, KHONG LAS DPON DU BSKOS, SPYI KHANG PHAL CHER GRUB
ZIN PA NA, KHONG SKU KHAMS MI BDE BA ZHIG

BSNYEN SGRUB ZLA BA BZHI LHAG MDZAD PAS NAD

GNYEN NYE GROGS PO RNAMS DANG MNYAM

DGOS BSAM PA YIN ZHUS, GONG MAS

DKA' SPYAD TSAD MED MYONG YANG CI MI

LO (1810) LA SKU BLTAMS, 'KHRUNGS NAS YUN RING MA SONG BAR SGAR
PA MNGA' RIS SPRUL SKU NAS TSE DBANG

ZHIG BSKUR TE SKU TSE YUN DU BRTAN PA'I RTEN 'BREL MDZAD, MCHOD
GNAS BLA MA GRAGS PA RAB BRTAN GYIS

'JAM DPAL ZLA BA ZHES PA'I MTSAN GSOL, MI RING BAR DGA' LDAN
KHRI THOG NGA GSUM PA RGYAL MTSAN SENG

GE'I YANG SPRUL DER PHEBS PA MJAL BAS BYIS PA 'DI THAR SHUL CHOS
SKYONG RGYA MTSO'I YANG SPRUL YIN ZHES LUNG

BSTAN, PHYIS SU PAn CHEN BSTAN PA'I NYI MAR THUGS BRTAGS ZHUS
PAS SPRUL SKU 'KHRUL MED YIN PAR THAG

BCAD, DGUNG LO LNGA PA TZAM NAS DGE BSHES CHEN PO NGAG DBANG
BZOD PA KLOG GI SLOB DPON DU BSTEN

NAS YI GE 'BRI KLOG DANG CHOS SPYOD SKOR RNAMS BLOR 'DZIN GYI
DBU BTZUGS, DGUNG LO BDUN BZHES PA

NA, DGE 'DUN YAR 'PHEL GYI DRUNG DU DGE BSNYEN DANG DGE TSUL GYI
SDOM PA DKYUS GCIG TU BSGRUBS,

MTSAN DGE 'DUN CHOS SKYONG RGYA MTSOR GSOL, DGUNG LO BCU BZHI
PAR BDE CHEN DGE TSOGS GLING DU PHEBS

NAS DGE 'DUN 'DUS PAR MANG 'GYED DANG BSNYEN BKUR ZHUS TE CHOS
GRVAR ZHUGS, KLOG GI SLOB DPON DE

NYID 'CHAD NYAN GYI YONGS 'DZIN DU BSTEN NAS RGYAL BA'I GSUNG
RAB RNAMS LA THOS BSAM MDZAD, NYIN MTSAN

KHOR MO YUG TU BRTZON PA CHU BO'I RGYUN BZHIN MDZAD DE RING MIN
GZHUNG POD LNGA'I DGONGS DON MA LUS PA THUGS

SU CHUD, DE DANG MNYAM DU DGE BSHES BSTAN PA DAR RGYAS MDUN NAS
SKAR RTZIS DANG, NYA MO RAB 'BYAMS

PA'I MDUN NAS SGRA DBYANGS CAN MA'I RI MO, GZHAN YANG SNYAN NGAG
GSO RIG SOGS THA SNYAD RIG PA'I GNAS

KUN LA'ANG SBYANGS PA MTHIL PHYIN MDZAD, DGUNG LO NYI SHU PAR
RJE NGAG DBANG BSTAN 'DZIN SPYAN SNGAR DGE SLONG

GI SDOM PA MNOS, DGUNG LO NYER GCIG PAR, SPYAN SNGA TSUL KHRIMS
'BAR GYI SPRUL SKU LA MO BLO GROS RGYA MTSOS

BTAB PA'I MGUR DGON RNAM RGYAL GLING GI GDAN KHRIR PHEBS, DGON
PA'I SGRIG LAM KUN SPYOD, CHO GA PHYAG

LEN TSANG MA NYAMS PA SOR CHUD MI NYAMS GONG 'PHEL SGO NAS LEGS
PAR BSKYANGS, DGUNG LO NYER BZHI PAR

RANG NYID KYI GDAN SA BDE CHEN CHOS GLING DU 'CHAD NYAN GYI 'GAN
KHUR BZHES TE BYANG CHUB LAM GYI RIM PA SOGS

BSHAD CING, CHOS SRID GNYIS THAD NAS DGON PA'I KHUR BZHES PAS,
GRVA TSOGS RGYAS SHING THOS BSAM 'CHAD

NYAN GYI BYA BA DAR RGYAS SU PHYIN, LHA RAMS PA BYAMS PA PHAN
BDE, RJE NGAG DBANG BSTAN 'DZIN SOGS GZHUNG

BRGYA SMRA BA'I MKHAS DBANG DU MA'I SPYAN SNGAR DAM CHOS ZAB

DAM PA'I CHOS KYIS BRLAN TE SGRUB PA SNYING POR BYED PA'I DGONGS
PA RNAL MAR 'CHAR, SKABS SHIG DPAL MANG

DKON MCHOG RGYAL MTSAN MDUN CHOS ZHU BA'I CHED DU BLA BRANG BKRA

GCIG RGYAL PO RANG GI GZIM KHANG DU BSHAMS NAS MCHOD, GCIG KHONG
LA GNANG BA CHU BZANG RI KHROD DU

BZHUGS, DGUNG LO NGA LNGAR PHEBS SKABS GONG MA YUNG tING LA RANG
YUL DU 'BYON RGYU'I DGONGS PA ZHUS,

GONG MAS RANG YUL DU LO GNYIS BZHUGS CHOG PA'I DGONGS KHROL
BYUNG, PHEBS PAR NYE BA NA, GONG MA YUNG

tING SKU GSHEGS, RGYAL SRAS BZHI PA CHEN LUNG RGYAL KHRIR
BZHUGS, CHEN LUNG MDUN SNGAR BZHIN RANG YUL DU

PHEBS RGYU'I DGONGS PA ZHUS PAS, DGONGS PA KHROL ZHING, DNGUL
DNGOS RGYA CHEN PO DANG, SKYEL MI CAR GU CHI

GCIG DMAG MI KHA SHAS, KHAL 'GEL DRE'U BRGYAD CU BCAS GNANG, DE
NAS MI RING BAR PE CING NAS BTEG

PE CING GI BLA DPON CHE PHRA TSANG MAS PHEBS SKYEL RGYA CHEN
MDZAD DE RIM GYIS MDO SMAD DGON LUNG DU BDE BAR

PHEBS, DGON LUNG GTZOS PA'I MDO SMAD KYI DGON CHE CHUNG TSANG
MAR MANG 'GYED DANG SPYI 'JOG BLA MA LAS

SNE, MTSO SNGON GYI DPON KHAG THAMS CAD LA GNANG SKYES PHUN SUM
TSOGS PA BSTZAL, DGON LUNG DGON PA'I

RGYAB RI LA RI KHROD CIG GSAR DU BTAB NAS SKU TSE MTHA' MA'I
BZHUGS GNAS MDZAD, DGUNG LO NGA BDUN DU

PHEBS PA RAB BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I ME 'BRUG LO (1736) ZLA BA
GNYIS PA'I TSES GSUM PA'I THO RANGS KYI DUS

GYIS SHING PAR GSAR DU BRKOS, RGYUD

BZHI'I DGONGS 'GREL <<BEE d'URA SNGON PO>> DANG, MAN NGAG RGYUD

<<LHAN THABS>> BOD KYI GSO RIG SKOR GYI LO RGYUS <<KHOG 'BUB
DRANG SRONG DGYES PA'I DGA' STON>> BCAS SNGA PHYIR

GSAR DU BRTZAMS, SMAN GZHUNG LE'U CHIG BRGYA NGA DRUG GI NANG
DON CHA TSANG GO RIM DANG LDAN PAR BRIS PA'I

SMAN DPE'I THANG GA BDUN CU DON DGU GSAR DU BZHENGS, GNA' RABS
SU BOD KYI GSO BA RIG PA 'DI LA

PHAL PA'I SPYOD YUL LAS 'DAS PA'I LHA SGRUNG LTA BU'I SENG RAS
KYIS G-YOGS PA BSAL TE, DON DNGOS DANG SBREL

NAS SLOB KHRID BYED PA'I SROL BZANG PO SPEL, DE NAS BZUNG KHAMS
SDE DGE DPAL SPUNGS DANG, MDO SMAD BLA

BRANG BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL SOGS DBUS GTZANG KHAMS GSUM DU BOD KYI
GSO BA RIG PA'I GZHUNG LUGS DANG, SMAN

PA MKHAS PA DBYAR MTSO RGYAS PA LTAR 'PHEL RGYAS SU PHYIN, RTZIS
RIG PA'I SKOR LA, BOD SNGAR YOD KYI RTZIS

YANG MDZAD DE, RTZIS GZHUNG <<BEE d'URA

DKAR PO>> DANG <<BEE d'URA G-YA' SEL>> <<DKA' GNAD SGO LCAGS
DBYE BA'I LDE MIG>> SOGS YID RTON TSAD MAR

GZUNG CHOG PA'I LEGS BSHAD MANG PO BRTZAMS, GZHAN YANG SNYAN
NGAG  SGRA, BZO, ZLOS GAR SOGS THA SNYAD

RIG PA'I BSTAN BCOS KYANG SNYAN ZHING 'JEBS PA 'GA' BRTZAMS TE
RANG CAG PHYI RABS PA DAG LA NAM YANG

BRJED DU MED PA'I MDZAD RJES BZHAG YOD, RAB BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I
LCAGS SBRUL LO (1701) LA BSTAN 'DZIN

DBANG RGYAL 'DAS PAR BRTEN SDE SRID MCHOG NAS LHA BZANG KHANG
DBUS SU BOS TE BOD SDOD SOG RGYAL GYI GO

SAR BZHAG PA RED, LHA BZANG GIS SOG RGYAL GYI GO MING 'DZIN NAS
BZUNG SDE SRID SANGS RGYAS RGYA MTSOR RGOL

BA'I 'KHRUG RTZOD KHO NA BSLANGS, KHOS SDE SRID 'DIS RNYING MA

MI 'DUG CES DANG, BSTAN 'DZIN DBANG RGYAL DUG GIS BSAD PA RED

LA BRTEN NAS SE 'BRAS DGE GSUM DANG SDE SRID BAR DBYEN DKRUG
BYAS, THA NA LHA BZANG GIS LKOG GSOD PA

'GA' ZHIG BTANG NAS SDE SRID KYI DRUNG 'KHOR DMAR BSAD BTANG BA
SOGS GDUG RTZUB KYI BYA NGAN MANG PO

BRTZAMS TE DBUS LHA LDAN GYI GNAS TSUL HA CANG MI BDE BAR GYUR,
RAB BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I SHING BYA LO'I SMON

LAM CHEN MO'I SKABS SU BDE 'JAGS DANG, LHA BZANG MI NGAN 'DI
DBUS NAS BSKRAD PA'I CHED DU, TA' LA'I

THAG BCAD, DE NAS LHA BZANG KHANG LA SDE SRID BKRONGS NAS BOD

NAS, BYANG NAG CHUR SLEBS MA THAG DE GAR SOG

RDZONG DU PHEBS, SOG DMAG GIS GNAS TSUL

RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS NYUNG BSDUS,...

PAn CHEN SKU PHRENG DANG PO MKHAS GRUB DGE LEGS DPAL BZANG NI
LI YUL LCANG RA SMUG PO NAS 'ONGS

PA'I SE'I RIGS KYI BRGYUD PA YAB KUN DGA' BKRA SHIS DPAL BZANG

@477

SRAS SU RAB BYUNG DRUG PA'I SHING MO GLANG GI LO(1385)LA LA STOD
BYANG GI SA CHAR SKU BLTAMS, GZHON NU NYID

NAS BYIS PA THA MAL PA'I SPYOD PA LAS RING DU BSRINGS TE NGAM
RING DANG, SA SKYA SOGS SU PHEBS NAS SDE SNOD

'DZIN PA'I MKHAS PA MANG PO'I DBUS SU MTSAN NYID THEG PA'I
GZHUNG LUGS LA GSAN SBYONG YANG DAG PAR

MDZAD, MKHYEN RAB THOGS PA MED PA'I BLO GROS KYI RTZAL DANG LDAN
PAS MKHAS PA RNAMS KYI YID PHROGS TE SNYAN

PA'I GRAGS PA THOB, MKHAS GRUB SENG GE RGYAL MTSAN BZANG POS
MKHAN PO DANG, RGYAL BA YON TAN 'OD KYIS

SLOB DPON MDZAD NAS DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA BZHES, MTSAN MKHAS GRUB
DGE LEGS DPAL BZANG GSOL,

SKABS DER NGAM RING DU BO DONG PAn CHEN 'JIGS BRAL PHYOGS LAS
RNAM RGYAL GYIS RIGS GTER NANG 'GAL GYI

PHUNG PO 'DI NGAS DGAG PAR BYED PA YIN PAS KHYED SA SKYA PA
RNAMS GROS KYIS LA LAN THOB GSUNGS NAS RIM

BZHIN BKAG PAS, DE DUS SA SKYA PA'I DGE BSHES SUS KYANG LAN
MDZAD MA NUS PA NA, RJE 'DI NYID DGUNG LO

BCU DRUG GI SKABS YIN YANG NGAS LAN BYED GSUNGS NAS DNGOS
STOBS KYI RIGS PA DANG DRI MA MED PA'I LUNG

GIS BO DONG PAn CHEN GYI RGOL LAN NAN SMIN MDZAD DE RIM BZHIN
YI GER BKOD, BO DONG PAn CHEN YANG THUGS

YID 'PHROGS TE BUNG BA RNAM PAR RTZEN PA'I RGYUD MANGS ZHES
BYA BA'I BSTOD PA PHUN SUM TSOGS PA ZHIG KYANG

MDZAD, SHING MO LUG GI SMIN DRUG ZLA BAR MKHAS DBANG RED MDA'
BA GZHON NU BLO GROS KYIS MKHAN PO MDZAD

DE BSNYEN PAR RDZOGS PA'I DGE SLONG GI SDOM PA MNOS, KHONG GI
DRUNG NAS DBU TSAD, 'DUL BA, MNGON PA, PHAR

PHYIN SOGS DKA' CHEN RNAMS KYI GZHI BSHAD RNAMS GSAN, GZHAN
YANG MKHAS GRUB SENG GE RGYAL MTSAN SOGS

BLA MA MANG POS DPAL LDAN SA SKYA'I RING LUGS KYIS GTZO BYAS
PA'I RIS SU MA CHAD PA'I GRUB MTHA' KUN GSAN

SBYONG MDZAD, DE'I TSE RJE BTZUN TZONG KHA PA CHEN PO'I SNYAN
PA'I GRAGS PA RGYA BOD HOR GSUM DU KHYAB PAR GSAN

NAS DGUNG LO NYER GSUM DU PHEBS SKABS RJE BTZUN RED MDA' BA
CHEN POS MTSAMS SBYOR MDZAD DE, RJE TZONG

KHA PA MJAL BAR DBUS LA PHEBS, SKABS DER RJE TZONG KHA PA SE
RA CHOS SDINGS SU DBYAR GNAS MDZAD NAS

BZHUGS YOD PAS THOG MAR DGE SLONG ZHI DUL CAN ZHIG DANG MJAL
BAR RJE TZONG KHA PA'I GZIM KHANG GANG DU

YOD CES DRI BA GNANG SKABS, DGE SLONG DES LAN MI SMRA BAR NANG
DU PHYIN NAS SPOS RING GCIG SPAR NAS BYUNG

STE GZIM KHANG SER PO'I MDUN DU SLEBS PA DANG PHYAG GSUM 'TSAL
NAS LAG GNYIS KYIS SPOS RING BZUNG SDE

BDAG NYID MKHAN PO RIN PO CHE BLO BZANG GRAGS PA'I ZHAL SNGA
NAS BZHUGS PA'I GTZUG LAG KHANG 'DI'O ZHES

SPOS RING BTZUGS PA DANG, 'DUL BA NAS BSHAD PA'I DGE SLONG GI
RTAGS CHA LUGS RNAMS LEGS PAR TSANG BA

SPYOD LAM DUL BA ZHIG YOD PAR GZIGS PA DANG BDAG NYID NA BZA'
PHU THUNG CAN BZHES PA SOGS MI CHEN GYI

CHA LUGS DANG LDAN ZHING, SNGAR MKHAS PA SUS KYANG 'GRAN PA'I
ZLA DANG BRAL BA'I STOBS KYIS THUGS NGA RGYAL

BA'I RNAM PA CAN YOD PAS THUGS LA 'TSER BA 'KHRUNGS TE DPA'
ZHUM PAR MDZAD, DE NAS RJE TZONG KHA PA MJAL

PAn CHEN SKU PHRENG BZHI PA BLO BZANG CHOS KYI RGYAL MTSAN NI,
GTZANG RONG GI MTSAMS LHAN GYI NANG DRUG

BRGYA ZHES PA'I SA GNAS SU PHYI CHAR YAB 'TSO BYED TSE RING
DPAL 'BYOR DU GRAGS KYANG DON LA GSO RIG GI YON

TAN DANG LDAN PA MES PO DRUNG 'TSO BA KUN DGA' 'OD ZER ZHES
BYA BA DANG, YUM MTSO RGYAL GNYIS KYI SRAS SU

RAB BYUNG BCU PA'I ME YOS(1567)LOR SKU BLTAMS, MTSAN LA CHOS
RGYAL DPAL LDAN BZANG PO ZHES GSOL

BYIS PA'I DUS NAS BAG YOD TSUL LDAN GYI SPYOD TSUL DANG, DGE
BA'I LAS SOGS CHOS SNANG LA MNGON PAR

DGYES SHING THOG MAR MKHAS GRUB SANGS RGYAS YE SHES KYI MDUN
NAS MDO SNGAGS KYI DBANG LUNG LEGS PAR

GSAN, DGUNG LO BCU GSUM DU SON SKABS KHYIM NAS THON TE DBEN SA
CHOS KYI PHO BRANG DU PHYAG BTEGS,

@497

MKHAS GRUB CHEN PO DE YIS MKHAN SLOB ZUNG 'BREL MDZAD NAS
TSIGS SNGA MA DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA LEGS PAR

THOB CING BLO BZANG CHOS KYI RGYAL MTSAN ZHES PA'I MTSAN
GNANG, DGUNG LO BCU BZHI'I DUS DBYANGS CAN LHA

MO'I BSTOD PA LHA'I GLU DBYANGS ZHES PA SNYAN TSIG PHUN SUM
TSOGS PA'I RGYAN DANG LDAN PA ZHIG BRTZAM PAR MDZAD

DE PHYAG BRIS SU BKOD, BLA MA'I BKA' BZHIN LAM RIM 'BRING BA
BZUNG NAS ZHAG BCU SKOR SONG MTSAMS LAM

RIM CHE BA BKLAGS PAS YONGS RDZOGS THUGS LA BZUNG STE RGYUGS
KYANG THOGS MED DU PHUL, DGUNG LO BCU DRUG

GI SKABS SU, MGON PO ZHI BA LHA'I RTOGS BRJOD PADMA DKAR PO'I
PHRENG BA ZHES SNYAN TSIG GIS BRGYAN PA ZHIG

KYANG BRTZAMS, ME KHYI LOR CHOS GRVA CHEN PO BKRA SHIS LHUN
POR PHYAG BTEGS, SKABS DER DGON GYI BLA SLOB

THAMS CAD KYIS PHYAG DANG BSNYEN BKUR GYIS MTHONG ZOS CHE BA
BYUNG, DE NAS GZHUNG POD RNAMS GO RIM LDAN

PA'I GSAN SBYONG LEGS PAR GNANG STE RIG CHEN PA'I KHROD DU DAM
BCA' DANG, BGRO GLENG MTHAR PHYIN PAR

MDZAD, LO DE'I ZLA BA BCU GCIG PAR MKHAS GRUB SANGS RGYAS YE
SHES SKU GSHEGS, DBEN DGON DU PHEBS TE

GDUNG RTEN LEGS PAR BZHENGS, SLAR BKRA SHIS LHUN POR PHEBS NAS
MKHAN RIN PO CHE PAn CHEN DAM CHOS

YAR 'PHEL GYI MDUN NAS BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI SDOM PA MNOS, STON
MJUG DBUS PHYOGS SU BYON TE RI BO DGE

LDAN DU MDO SNGAGS YONGS RDZOGS KYI DGE BSHES BRGYA PHRAG MANG
PO DANG, SDE PA SKYID SHOD PA SOGS SER SKYA

'DU TSOGS CHE BA'I DBUS SU CHOS RJE KHRI PA'I BKA' BZHIN DBU
MA DANG, TSAD MA GNYIS KYIS GTZOS BKA'

POD KYI DAM BCA' GLO BUR DU 'JOG GNANG MDZAD DGOS BYUNG YANG,
THOGS PA MED CING PHYOGS LAS RGYAL BA'I

GRAGS PA THOB, GNAS DER SLOB DPON RIN PO CHE MKHYEN RAB DBANG
PHYUG DANG, RJE BTZUN NAM MKHA' RGYAL

MTSAN, SLOB DPON DGE 'DUN RGYAL MTSAN, RNAM RGYAL DPAL BZANG
SOGS KYI MDUN NAS MDO SNGAGS KYI

GZHUNG LUGS CI RIGS GSAN, DGUNG LO SUM CU LA NYE SKABS RJE
BKRAS RIG PA SOGS DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN

DU MAR DBANG LUNG KHRID GSUM GYI CHOS BKA' MANG DU BSTZAL, DE
NAS SDE PA LHUN RTZE PA DANG, MCHOD YON

THAMS CAD KYIS NAN GYIS BSKUL BAR BRTEN NAS GANGS CAN CHOS
'PHEL DGON GYI MKHAN PO'I KHRI THOG TU BZHUGS,

DGON SDE'I GTZUG LAG KHANG NYAMS GOG TU SONG BA RNAMS LEGS PAR
GSOS, DE NAS BKRAS LHUN SPYI SOS JI

LTAR SKUL BA BZHIN LCAGS GLANG LO CHOS GRVA CHEN PO DER PHEBS
NAS GDAN KHRIR 'KHOD, SKABS SHIG DBUS SU

PHEBS TE LHA SA DANG RA SGRENG, 'PHAN PO, LHO KHUL, GTZANG
STOD SOGS GANG SAR GNAS MJAL DU BYON, DKON

MCHOG LA MCHOD 'BUL DGE 'DUN LA BSNYEN BKUR SOGS SKYE BO SER
SKYA MANG POR CHOS SBYIN RGYA CHEN POS RE BA

BSKONG BAR MDZAD, BAR SKABS SHIG TU BKRAS LHUN DGON GYI GRVA
TSANG PHAN TSUN RTZOD GZHI DANG, 'THAB

'DZINGS SOGS CI RIGS BYUNG BA'I 'BYUNG PO'I RGYU LAM GYI DRA
BA GCOD THABS SU DBYEN 'DUMS MCHOD RTEN  

ZHIG BZHENGS PAR MDZAD RJES DGE 'DUN RNAMS THUGS MTHUN BSHAD
SGRUB KYI 'CHAD NYAN 'PHEL BA SOGS BYUNG,

'BRAS SPUNGS NAS GDAN ZHU'I PHO NYA 'BYOR BA LTAR SLAR YANG
DBUS SU PHEBS TE RGYAL BA YON TAN RGYA MTSO DANG,

SER 'BRAS KYI BLA MA SLOB DPON RNAMS LA RDO RJE PHRENG BA'I
DBANG YONGS RDZOGS PHUL NAS GTZANG PHYOGS SU

@498

PHEBS, DE NAS MON PHYOGS SU ZHABS BTEGS, SPYIR LHO MON 'DI
BZHIN RANG RANG GI GRUB MTHA' DANG BLA MA

SO SO'I PHYOGS ZHEN GZHAN LAS CHE YANG BDAG NYID CHEN PO 'DIS
CHAGS SDANG NGAN PA'I GRUB MTHA'I PHYOGS RIS

MI 'DZIN PAR BRTEN TSANG MAS BSNYEN BKUR DANG, ZHABS TOG TSAD
MED BYAS, LHAG PAR GSOD RES DANG,

DGRA SHA LEN PAR CHAS PA'I MI RNAMS LA DNGOS PO'I SBYIN PA
SNGON DU 'GRO BA'I SGO NAS PHRENG BA SPYI BOR BZHAG STE

DGRA SHA MI LEN PA'I DAM BCA' BZHAG NAS BDE 'JAGS SU GNAS PA
SOGS BSTAN PA DANG, SEMS CAN LA

PHAN PA RGYA CHEN PO BSGRUBS, DE'I TSE RGYAL BA RIN PO CHES MI
SNA CHED STZAL BZHIN LHA SAR PHEBS TE SMON LAM

CHEN MO'I TSOGS DBU KUN TU MDZAD, SPRUL SKU BSOD NAMS DGE LEGS
DPAL BZANG SOGS DGE BSHES BZHI

BCU TZAM LA BSNYEN RDZOGS DANG, MI STONG PHRAG BRGAL BAR RAB
BYUNG GI SDOM PA BSTZAL, LO DE'I STON MJUG

TU SOG DMAG BYANG RGYUD DU SLEBS PAR SDE SRID DPON BLON GYI
BKA' BKOD BZHIN CHINGS LUGS MDZAD PAR

PHEBS TE MI DU MA'I SROG DBANG SKYOB PAR MDZAD, RGYAL BA YON
TAN RGYA MTSO'I MCHOG SPRUL RIN PO CHE 'BRAS  

SPUNGS SU SPYAN DRANGS, GTZUG PHUD BZHES TE BLO BZANG RGYA MTSO
ZHES PA'I MTSAN GSOL, RDO RJE PHRENG BA'I DBANG

YONGS RDZOGS PHUL TE BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI MKHAN PO MDZAD, SOG
DMAG GTZANG DU SLEBS PAR LDOG THABS SU

PHEBS DGOS PA'I BKA' BZHIN BYON, SOG PO RNAMS SPE SNGON NA GA
ZHES PA'I SA GNAS SU BABS YOD PAS

MTHONG STE RTA BA BRGYA TZAM ZHIG LHAGS TE SKU DBANG MED PAR
SOG KHROD DU GDAN DRANGS PAR PHEBS DGOS BYUNG

BA LAS, SA SKYONG MI'I DBANG POR SKYON CHAGS PA'I DGONGS BSAM
LOG PA CI LA MNGA', 'ON KYANG BKRA SHIS

LHUN PO'I NYE 'DABS SU DGON PA ZHIG GSAR RGYAG THOG MING
LA'ANG BKRA SHIS ZIL GNON ZHES BTAGS PA SOGS

KYI GNAS TSUL BYUNG, DE NAS DPAL 'KHOR BDE CHEN DANG, SNAR
THANG SOGS RIS MED CHOS SDE KHAG GI MKHAN

DBYANGS RGYA MTSO MCHOG RGYA YUL DU PHEBS DGOS

BYUNG BA MTSO KHAR ZHING DU GSHEGS RJES ME PHAG LO RGYAL PO
NAS BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I MCHOD GZHIS SU RTA NAG RIN

RTZE SOGS SBYOR 'JAGS THOG  SPRUL PA'I SKUR RAB BYUNG BSNYEN
RDZOGS SOGS 'BUL BA'I MKHAN POR PAn CHEN

RIN PO CHE PHEBS DGOS LUGS GSUNG NAN LTAR DBUS SU PHEBS, PO TA
LA'I TSOM CHEN SRID ZHI PHUN TSOGS SU

THOG MA'I ZHAL 'DZOMS, DE NAS LHA LDAN GTZUG LAG KHANG DU JO
BO SH'AKYA MU NE'I SPYAN SNGAR BDAG NYID CHEN

POS MKHAN SLOB ZUNG SBREL MDZAD NAS RGYAL BA'I SPRUL SKUR DGE
BSNYEN NAS BZUNG BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI DNGOS PO

DKYUS THOG GCIG TU PHUL NAS NGAG DBANG YE SHES RGYA MTSO ZHES
PA'I MTSAN GSOL, 'JIGS BYED SKYED RDZOGS

KYI LUNG DANG, DE MIN RJES GNANG SOGS 'BUL GNANG GIS SLAR BKRA
SHIS LHUN POR PHYIR PHEBS, ME BYA LO

JUN GAR HONG THA'I JI'I DMAG PHON CHE BA NAG TSANG PHYOGS SU
'BYOR SKAD DANG, RGYAL PO LHA BZANG GIS 'DAM

DU SOG BOD HOR BCAS KYI DPUNG DMAG KHYON CHE BA BSAGS NAS YOD
SKAD LA PHAN TSUN THAL CHA MI 'BYUNG CHED

BDAG NYID CHEN PO SGAR SAR CHINGS DAN MDZAD PAR CHIBS BSKYOD,
RGYAL PO DANG JUN GAR BA'I DMAG DPON

RNAMS LA PHAN TSUN 'THAB 'DZING MED PAR BAR CHINGS LA DAN DGOS
LUGS RIM BSTUD KYIS NAN GSUNG MDZAD

KYANG, JUN GAR BA'I DMAG DPON RNAMS NAS BRJOD GSAL RGYAL PO
DANG, JUN GAR BA'I DMAG DPON TSE

RING DON GRUB GNYIS NGO BSHER BYUNG NA MA GTOGS DE MIN BRJOD
BDE MED LUGS SOGS LABS PA TZAM LAS,

BAR CHINGS SKOR 'DI BYED LAN GSAL MED PA DANG BCAS RGYAL PO
YANG 'DAM NAS PHYIR PHEBS, MI RING BAR JUN

GAR BA'I DMAG RNAMS GRONG SMAD DANG, GLANG RU, RKYANG THANG
SGANG GSUM LA SGAR PHAB, YANG BSKYAR PHAN TSUN

GNYIS KAR 'THAB 'DZING MED PA'I ZHU CHINGS NAN CHE MDZAD KYANG
LUGS 'GRIG MA BYUNG BAR MTHAR RGYAL PO DPON

G-YOG PO TA LA ZHOL NAS PHYIR THON MDZAD SKABS JUN GAR BA'I
DMAG MIS RGYAL PO NGO MA SHES PAR MTSON THAL

GYIS BKRONGS, DPON MO SRAS BCAS SROG SKYON MI YONG BA ZHU SNA
MDZAD DE PO TA LAR PHEBS, JUN GAR BA'I

@508

'GO DMAG RNAMS LA MJAL KHA DGOS LUGS BZHIN 'GO DMAG BZHI STONG
SKOR LA BSNYEN GNAS NYIN ZHAG GCIG

PA'I SDOM PA GNANG, DE NAS MI RING BAR BKRA SHIS LHUN POR
PHYIR PHEBS, CHOS GRVA 'DIR RJE DGE 'DUN GRUB

PA NAS BSTZAL BA'I BCA' YIG RIN PO CHE'I DGONGS DON LTAR BSLAB
PA GSUM GYI NYAMS BZHES LA KHYAD PAR MI

CHE YANG 'PHRAL GYI SGRIGS LAM 'GA' ZHIG SO SO'I SROL RGYUN
BZHIN GDAN SA CHEN PO BZHI RNAMS CUNG MTHUN MIN

RIGS CHA MTHUN GYI BCA' YIG ZHIG KYANG GTAN LA PHAB, ZHVA LU
DGON GYI SLOB DPON LAS BYED DANG, TSOGS

DMANGS MGRIN GCIG NAS GSOL BA BTAB DON BZHIN DGON DE'I MKHAN
PO GNANG RGYUR ZHAL BZHES MDZAD, SMAD

PHYOGS SU RGYA DANG, MTSO KHA'I DMAG PHON CHE YOD TSUL BYUNG
BA RNAMS DANG JUN GAR BA GNYIS PHAN TSUN 'THAB

'DZINGS SU MA SONG BA'I MTHUN SBYOR GANG ZAB DGOS LUGS KYI
BKA' MCHID DANG SBRAGS MI SNA CHED RDZONG MDZAD

PAR SO PA PHAN TSUN 'THAB PA TZAM LAS, ZING CHA CHE RIGS MA
BYUNG BAR JUN GAR BA'I DPON JA'I SANG DMAG

DANG BCAS GNAM MTSO BRGYUD JUN GAR DU 'BYON PAR THAG CHOD,
SLAR YANG BKRA SHIS LHUN PO NAS DBUS SU

BYON, PO TA LAR GONG SA RIN PO CHE SKU PHRENG BDUN PA DANG
ZHAL 'DZOMS THOG  GONG MA'I MI SNA DANG CANG CUN

BCAS NAS GONG MAS BSTZAL BA'I GSER YIG DANG, RTEN CHAS BCAS
GNANG BA DGYES BZHES MDZAD, GONG SA

MCHOG LA DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA 'BUL GNANG THOG MTSAN SNGAR YOD
THOG BLO BZANG ZHES PA KHA SNON DU PHUL NAS BLO

BZANG SKAL BZANG RGYA MTSO ZHES MTSAN GSOL BA MA ZAD, DE NAS
RIM BZHIN BDAG NYID CHEN POS MKHAN PO

DANG, DGA' LDAN KHRI PA DPAL LDAN GRAGS PAS LAS SLOB, RGYUD
SMAD MKHAN PO NGAG DBANG CHOS LDAN GYIS

GSANG STON BCAS MDZAD DE BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI SDOM PA 'BUL BZHES
THOG  SNGA PHYIR MDO SNGAGS KYI DBANG LUNG SNA

TSOGS KYANG 'BUL GNANG MDZAD PA SOGS CHOS 'BREL GYI SLOB MAR
GYUR PA SKYES BU DAM PA JI SNYED CIG BYUNG

YOD LA, SKYE BO SER SKYA GRANGS LAS 'DAS PAR DAM PA'I CHOS KYI
'KHOR LO ZAM MI CHAD PAR BSKOR BAR MDZAD

CING, DBUS GTZANG GI RIS MED DGON SDE KHAG LA MCHOD SPRIN
DANG, BSNYEN CING BKUR BA SOGS RE RE

BZHIN BRJOD KYI MI LANGS PA'I MKHAS BTZUN BZANG GSUM LDAN PA'I
GO 'PHANG DU MNGA' RNYED, KHONG GI SKU TSE'I

DUS SKABS SU DA DUNG NGA LUM SBYAR GSUM DANG, PHO LHA THA'I JI
SOGS PHAN TSUN NANG 'GAL CHE BA'I BDE GZAR

GYI SKABS KYANG 'KHEL BAS BDAG NYID CHEN PO 'DIS ZHI 'GRIGS
'BYUNG THABS KYIS MTSON SKYE 'GRO RNAMS SDUG

BSNGAL SEL ZHING, BDE BAR GNAS THABS SOGS SKYES BU DAM PA'I
MDZAD PA RLABS PO CHES DUS 'DA' BAR

MDZAD DE RAB BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I ME SBRUL(1737)LO DGUNG
GRANGS BDUN CU DON LNGAR PHEBS SKABS ZHI

BAR GSHEGS,

KHONG GI GSUNG RAB KYI RNAM GRANGS, RANG RNAM SOGS RNAM THAR
DANG, SNYAN NGAG LE'U GNYIS PA'I DPE

BRJOD, THOB YIG  DKAR CHAG  SGRUB THABS DANG GSOL 'DEBS SKOR
CHOS TSAN MANG ZHIG MCHIS PA KA NAS

PAn CHEN DRUG PA DPAL LDAN YE SHES NI, GTZANG GI SA'I CHA
SHANGS BKRA SHIS RTZE ZHES PAR YAB THANG

LHA DANG, YUM NYI ZLA DBANG MO GNYIS KYI SRAS SU RAB BYUNG BCU
GNYIS PA'I SA RTA LO(1738)ZLA BA BCU GCIG

PA'I TSES BCU GCIG LA SKU BLTAMS, SKU NA CHUNG NGU'I DUS NAS
BYIS PA PHAL PA'I SPYOD PA MTHA' DAG LAS NI

RGYAB KYIS PHYOGS, DAD PA DANG GTONG PHOD RANG BZHIN GYIS YID
GZHUNG BA SOGS YA RABS KYI SPYOD PA DU MAS

MDZES SHING, LCAGS SPREL LOR DGUNG LO GSUM LA PHEBS SKABS
RGYAL DBANG BSKAL BZANG RGYA MTSOS BLO BZANG

DPAL LDAN YE SHES ZHES PA'I MTSAN GSOL BA DANG SBRAGS BKRA
SHIS RTZER DGA' STON LEGS 'BUL ZHU BAR MI

SNA CHED DU MNGAGS, BKRA SHIS RTZE NAS, SHANGS LUG GI GDONG
GZHIS KA DON GRUB SMON KHAR DU SPYAN DRANGS,

DER MI DBANG PHO LHA'I SKU TSAB SOGS RTA PA BRGYA PHRAG BRGAL
BA GDAN SAR SPYAN 'DREN DU BYON, GZHIS KA DER

YOD PA'I PAn CHEN SKU GONG MA'I BZHUGS KHRI'I STENG DU SPYAN
DRANGS, DE NAS MTHONG SMON GSHONG DU BZHUGS ZHAG 

THOG  GONG MA'I SKU TSAB DANG, MI DBANG BSOD NAMS STOBS RGYAL,
RGYAL DBANG MCHOG GI SKU TSAB BCAS

PHEBS MJAL DU BCAR, DE SKABS SKU NA SHIN TU PHRA YANG SKYA SER
GYI TSOGS MANG DBUS SU BAG TSA BA DANG ZHUM

PA'I RNAM PA CUNG ZAD KYANG MI MNGA' ZHING GANG LA'ANG 'JIGS
PA MED PAR BZHUGS PAS, GONG MA'I MI SNA

SOGS THAMS CAD NGO MTSAR SKYES TE SKU BSOD CAN ZHIG 'ONG BA
'DUG CES GLENG, DE NAS RGYA BOD SOG GSUM

GYI RTA PA STONG PHRAG BRGAL BA'I PHEBS BSU DANG BCAS CHOS SDE
CHEN PO BKRA SHIS LHUN POR CHIBS BSGYUR MDZAD,

SLOB DPON MKHAS PA BSTEN NAS LJAGS KLOG SLOB PAR GNANG BAS YIG
KLOG SHIN TU BYANG BA DANG, GANG BLO MA

SOGS DPE CHA KHA SHAS DKA' TSEGS MED PAR LJAGS 'DZIN GRUB,
DGUNG LO LNGA LA SON BSKABS RJE NGAG DBANG

BYAMS PA'I DRUNG NAS BYANG CHUB LAM SGRON GYI LUNG SOGS MANG
PO GSAN SKABS, PHYAG DPE'I DBU SHOG PHYAG TU

PHUL BA SMRA BRJOD GTZANG ZHING SHAR RGYAG GIS KLOG PA GNANG
BAS BLA MA MCHOG KYANG THUGS DGYES, CHU PHAG LO

SNGAGS CHEN RDO RJE 'DZIN PA BLO BZANG BZOD PA YONGS 'DZIN DU
BSTEN NAS DBANG LUNG RJES GNANG SOGS MANG

PO GSAN, SHING BYI LOR GONG MA CHEN PO NAS PE CING DU YUNG HE
KUNG ZHES PA'I DGE 'DUN GYI SDE GSAR 'DZUGS

MDZAD PAR RJE NYID NAS BKA' DRIN CHE TSUL GYI ZHU YIG RTEN
LDAN BCAS 'BUL GNANG MDZAD, DGUNG LO BDUN

LA SON SKABS YONGS 'DZIN BLO BZANG BZOD PAS MKHAN PO DANG,
DKYIL KHANG BLO BZANG DON GRUB NAS SLOB

DPON, THOS BSAM GLING BLO BZANG MKHAS BTZUN NAS DUS GO BA SOGS
MDZAD NAS RAB TU BYUNG STE DGE TSUL GYI

SDOM PA BZHES, BOD KYI SRID SKYONG MI DBANG DANG, DGA' BZHI
GUNG SOGS NAS SPOS SNA DANG BCAS BKRA SHIS

LHUN PO'I GTZUG LAG KHANG CHEN POR 'PHAGS TSOGS 'DUS PA RGYA
MTSO'I DBUS SU SPRUL SKU NYID BSTAN 'GRO

YONGS KYI PHAN BDE'I BYED POR MNGA' GSOL, GONG MA NAS BSTZAL
BA'I RIN PO CHE'I SPYAD PA SOGS GNANG SKYES

SHAS KYIS BSKUL NGOR BLO GROS DPAG BSAM

MA DANG, BLO BZANG RGYAL BA'I RING LUGS MA TSIGS BCAD KYI
GSUNG GNYIS GSAR RTZOM MDZAD, GSUNG DE

GNYIS BKA' RTZOM GYI THOG MA YIN GSHIS TSIG SBYOR PHUN SUM
TSOGS PAS MKHAS PA RNAMS YID 'PHROG PAR BYED

PA ZHIG BYUNG NGO, ,RAB BYUNG BCU GSUM PA'I SA SBRUL LO LBANG
DA LAS B'A THUR GYIS GDAN ZHU BYAS PA BZHIN BKRA

'KHEL DGON SDE KHAG LA MCHOD SPRIN DANG,

BSNYEN BKUR MANG 'GYED SOGS GZAB RGYAS BSTABS TE RTZE PHO
BRANG CHEN POR ZHABS SOR 'KHOD NAS RGYAL BA

SOGS KYI DBANG LUNG MANG PO GSAN, CHU SPRE

KHANG PA BLO BZANG CHOS 'PHEL DGONGS PAR

CHEN POS RGYAL BA'I DBANG POR DBU MDZAD

'CHAM SLOB MI GNYIS BKRA SHIS LHUN PO NAS

BZANG DGE 'DUN DANG, DKA' CHEN BLO BZANG

RIM TSOGS DBUR PHEBS NAS BSDUS GRVA'I BGRO GLENG

THOG MAR MDZAD PA DANG CHABS CIG MTSAN NYID KYI GZHUNG LUGS
KHAG LA GO RIM LDAN PA'I SLOB GNYER LEGS

PAR BSKYANGS, ZUR BZHI'I SLOB DPON RNAMS DANG LHAN CIG TSAD MA
RNAM 'GREL GYI DGONGS DON BGRO GLENG

MDZAD PAS MKHYEN DPYOD KYI 'JUG PA DBYAR MTSO 'PHEL BA LA

LA'I BLA MA BSKAL BZANG RGYA MTSO MCHOG ZHI BAR GSHEGS PAS DE
'PHRAL DGONGS RDZOGS MCHOD 'BUL RGYA CHER

MDZAD, MCHOG SPRUL MYUR DU BYON PA'I GSOL 'DEBS SHIG KYANG
BRTZAMS, LO 'DIR YONGS 'DZIN BLO BZANG

CHOS 'PHEL GYIS MKHAN PO DANG, BSAM GLING BLO BZANG BKRA SHIS
KYIS LAS SLOB, SHAR RTZE BLO BZANG MKHAS

MCHOG GIS GSANG STON, DKYIL KHANG BLO BZANG BRTZON 'GRUS KYIS
DUS GO BA SOGS MDZAD NAS BSNYEN PAR

RDZOGS PA DGE SLONG GI SDOM PA MNOS, THUGS RDZOGS SU BZHES
PA'I DGA' STON DU GTZANG KHUL DGON KHAG SUM  

BRGYA LNGA BCU NGA BDUN DANG, SGRUB SDE SUM CU SO BZHI BCAS
PAR BSNYEN BKUR MANG 'GYED SOGS GZAB RGYAS

BSTABS, SGRUB BRGYUD BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME RJE NGAG DBANG BYAMS
PA BKRA SHIS LHUN POR GDAN DRANGS, BYANG CHUB

CHE'I DKAR CHAG BRTZAMS PAR MDZAD, DBUS

RAB GNAS LEGS PAR BSKYANGS TE GDAN SA RI BO DGA' LDAN DANG, RA
SGRENG SOGS LA GNAS GZIGS GNANG

NAS BKRA SHIS LHUN POR PHYIR PHEBS MDZAD, LCAGS SBRUL LOR T'A
LA'I BLA MA SKU PHRENG BDUN PA'I YANG SRID MCHOG

RIN PO CHER DBU SKRA GTZUG PHUD 'BUL BZHES

DPAL RGYA MTSO DPAL BZANG PO ZHES GSOL, RAB

MDZAD RGYU'I DUS SU BABS PAS THOG MAR CHAB MDO

SDOM PA BSTZAL, SHING SPRE LOR TSE DPAG MED KYI

LAS GRUB LA BRGYA DANG BRGYAD CU GYA BRGYAD,

KYIS RAB GNAS MDZAD, SHING BYA LOR DBUS

MDUN DU RGYAL BA 'JAM DPAL RGYA MTSOR DGE TSUL

GYI BSLAB SDOM 'BUL BA'I MKHAN PO MDZAD, SE 'BRAS DGE GSUM
DANG RGYUD GRVA STOD SMAD, DBUS KHUL LHO BYANG

DANG, MCHOD SPRIN RGYA CHE GZAB 'BUL THOG SKYE

BO SER SKYA MANG POR CHOS SBYIN GYIS TSIM PAR MDZAD, ME KHYI
LOR GONG MA'I SKU TSAB A'A SA HAN KAN AAM BAN

'JA' SA GSER THAM BCAS 'BUL

BSTAN PA SANGS RGYAS NAS RJE BTZUN MI LA'I RNAM

MGUR YONGS RDZOGS PAR DU BRKOS NAS BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I PAR
KHANG DU BZHUGS PAR DGYES PA CHEN POS

GZENGS BSTOD KYANG BSTZAL, CHU 'BRUG LO GONG MAS RGYU YON
SBYAR TE BKRA SHIS LI MA LAS BSGRUB PA'I TSE DPAG

MED KYI 'DRA SKU LNGA BCU NGA DRUG GSAR BZHENGS DGOS LUGS BOD
BZHUGS AAM BAN BRGYUD PAn CHEN RIN PO CHE

@598

RAB BYUNG BCU BZHI PA'I SA 'BRUG LO (1808) LA 'KHRUNGS, SKU
GZHON NU'I DUS NAS, GRUB BRGYA'I GTZUG RGYAN

RIG 'DZIN BYANG CHUB RDO RJE'I DRUNG DU RAB TU BYUNG, MTSAN AO
RGYAN 'JIGS MED CHOS DBANG ZHES GSOL,

KHONG SKU NA CHUNG NGU'I DUS NAS THEG PA CHEN PO'I RIGS SAD CING
SKYES THOB KYI MKHYEN PA THOGS MED MNGA' BAS

SLOB DPON GYIS JI SKAD GSUNGS PA KUN TSEGS MED DU MKHYEN, RIS
MED DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN MANG DU

BSTEN, RIG PA'I GNAS CHE PHRA KUN LA MKHYEN PA'I KLONG BRDOL,
GANGS CAN MKHAS DBANG KUN GYI GTZUG RGYAN

DU GYUR, BLA MA GONG MA'I RTOGS PA RGYUD LA 'PHOS PAS, NYAMS
RTOGS KHYAD PAR CAN THUGS LA 'KHRUNGS, SNYIGS

DUS GRUB THOB YONGS KYI RGYAL POR GYUR, DE LTA BU MKHAS GRUB
GNYIS LDAN GYI SKYES CHEN DAM PA 'DIS CHER RLOM

DANG KHENGS DREGS GTAN NAS MED PAR PHYI TSUL PHAL PAR MDZAD
CING, GSUNG RAB BRTZAMS PA HA CANG MANG

YANG RANG NYID KYIS GCIG KYANG TSAGS SU MA MDZAD, GSUNG RAB MANG
CHE BAR RTZOM PA PO'I MTSAN BKOD MED LA,

GSUNG RAB 'GA' ZHIG LA MJUG BYANG DU MING 'KHOD PA RNAMS KYANG
DPER NA, ``KHYI RGAN DPAL DGE, AA BU

HRAL PO, AA BU LHOD PO, KHYI RGAN AA BU,'' ZHES PA SOGS RANG
NYID DMA' SAR 'DZIN PA'I MING KHO NAR 'KHOD,

KHONG GI BRTZAMS CHOS TSANG MA BRDA RNYING DANG MNGON BRJOD MANG
PO MED CING TSIG SNYAN 'JEBS DANG LDAN PA,

BLTAS PA TZAM LA DON GSAL BAR GO NUS PA, NGO BSTOD DANG ZOL ZOG
GI TSIG GTAN NAS MED CING, GSUNG

RAB TSANG MA TSIG NYUNG ZHING DON 'DUS PA DANG, DKOR RDZAS LA
RNGAM ZHING LUNG RTOGS KYI YON TAN CI'ANG MED

PA'I BLA RDZUN CHEN POR RLOM PA DAG LA ZUR ZA'I TSIG DAG NI KHAB
LTAR RNO ZHING GNAD 'PHIGS PA'I RANG BZHIN

YOD, KHONG GI GSUNG RAB RNAMS SU MA RABS KYI NGAN SPYOD MTHA'
DAG LA RGOL ZHING, YA RABS KYI SPYOD PA LA

BSTOD PA DANG, G-YO SGYU SPANGS TE DRANG PO BYA RGYU 'DI NI MI
CHOS KYI MCHOG YIN PAR GSUNGS PA DPER NA,

KHONG GI GSUNG <<CHOS DANG 'JIG RTEN SHES PA'I BSTAN BCOS GDOL
PA'I DRANG SRONG GI GTAM THAR PA'I THEM SKAS>>

LAS ``DRANG PO DE YANG GANG ZHE NA, ,G-YO SMYU YONGS SU SPANGS
NAS NI, ,KHA DANG DON DU MTSUNGS PA DANG, ,PHYI

DANG NANG DU MTSUNGS PA'O, ,'' ZHES DANG DE'I 'BRU 'GREL DU
``KHA NI BRJOD PA'I GTAM YIN DON NI DE'I LAG LEN

YIN, PHYI NI LUS DANG NGAG YIN NANG NI RANG GI SEMS YIN,'' ZHES
DANG, MTHAR PHYOGS SDOM GYI SKABS SU,

``SEMS LA G-YO SMYU SPANGS NAS NI, ,DRANG PO'I SPYOD PA 'DI KHO
NA, ,MI YI CHOS LUGS MCHOG YIN TE, ,MI

CHOS THAMS CAD 'DI LA 'DUS, ,'' ZHES GSUNGS, DAM PA 'DI NYID NI,
NANG NYAMS RTOGS KYI DROD TSAD SHIN TU

MTHON POR GYUR KYANG, PHYI TSUL THOG RANG GI YON TAN LA MNGON
RLOM CUNG ZAD MED PAR SBAS SHING, RANG NYID

LA DMAN PA'I 'DU SHES KYI DMA' SA KHO NAR 'DZIN, GRUB MTHA' RIS
MED DAG LA GUS SHING DAG SNANG YUG

GCIG TU MDZAD PAS, GZUR BOR GNAS PA'I MKHAS PA KUN GYIS BSNGAGS
BRJOD BYAS, SLOB MA YANG GRUB

MTHA' RIS MED KYI BLA SPRUL MANG DU SPEL, KHAMS KYI MKHAS DBANG
'JU MI PHAM RGYA MTSOS KYANG KHONG SLOB DPON

DU BSTEN MYONG BA RED, RAB BYUNG BCO LNGA PA'I ME PHAG LO (1887)
LA SKU'I BKOD PA YONGS SU BSDUS SO, ,

KHONG GI GSUNG RAB RNAMS PHYOGS DANG PHYOGS SU THOR, PHYIS SU
KHONG GI DNGOS SLOB DGE MANG DPON

@599

AO RGYAN BSTAN 'DZIN NOR BUS, PHYOGS MTHA' DAG NAS JI LTAR RNYED
PA TSANG MA GCIG TU BSDUS TE GLEGS BAM

DRUG TU BKOD, YIG NOR JI YOD DAG PAR BCOS SHING YON SBYOR DANG
BCAS RGYAL SRAS SPRUL SKU GZHAN PHAN CHOS

KYI SNANG BA LA PAR DU 'GOD PA'I MGO 'DREN ZHUS PA BZHIN, SPRUL
PA'I SKU DE NYID KYIS PAR DU BSGRUBS, PAR

SHING DE DAG DA LTA BZHUGS MED PAR MNGON YANG PAR GZHI DER MA
PHYI BYAS TE 'PHRUL PAR BRGYABS PA'I PO TI

MKHAS DBANG DPAL MANG DKON MCHOG RGYAL MTSAN NI, MDO SMAD KYI

SHIS 'KHYIL GYI NYE 'KHOR LHO NGOS BSANG GZHUNG ZHES PAR RUS
TSAR TSA YIN PA'I YAB DBANG GRAGS SKYABS DANG 

@611

YUM BDE ZA LHA MO GNYIS KYI SRAS SU RAB BYUNG BCU GSUM PA'I
SHING SPREL(1764)LOR SKU BLTAMS, YAB YUM

GNYIS LA SRAS GSUM YOD PA'I YA GYAL CHUNG SHOS DE YIN, DGUNG
LO DRUG TU SON SKABS KUN MKHYEN BLA MA

DKON MCHOG 'JIGS MED DBANG PO'I DRUNG NAS RAB BYUNG BSGRUBS,
MTSAN DKON MCHOG RGYAL MTSAN ZHES PA

BSTZAL, RTZE GZHUNG DU DPAL MANG SKU GONG MA'I LHA GUR DU GDAN
DRANGS NAS KHRI LA BKOD, DGE SLONG BSAM

GTAN SENG GE KLOG GI SLOB DPON DU GDAN DRANGS, SLOB GNYER LA
BRTZON PAR MDZAD PAS PHRAL KLOG DANG,

SBYAR KLOG GNYIS KA MI RING BAR THUGS SU CHUD, CHOS SPYOD KHAG
RNAMS THUGS 'DZIN GNANG, DGUNG LO BCU

GCIG PAR LNGA MCHOD KYI TSOGS DBUS SU SA LAM SKABS GSUM MA'I
ZHAL 'DON DBU BSKUL DANG, BSNGO BA

BCAS MDZAD SKABS GSUNG GDANGS LEGS SHING, ZHUM PA'I RNAM 'GYUR
SPU TZAM MED PA SOGS KYIS THAMS CAD

DAD GUS TSAD MED SKYES, SOG YUL DU PHEBS TE ZLA SHAS TZAM NAS
DGON PAR PHYIR PHEBS, KHRI RIN PO CHE NGAG

DBANG 'PHRIN LAS KYIS DGE BSHES 'DUL BA 'DZIN PA RDO RAMS PA
TSUL KHRIMS SENG GE DGE RGAN DU BSKOS,

MTSAN NYID KYI GZHUNG LUGS LA SLOB GNYER GNANG STE MANG JA'I
TSOGS BAR DU BSDUS GRVA SHOG LHE GNYIS TZAM RE

THUGS 'DZIN MDZAD, DGUNG GRANGS BCU BZHIR SON PA'I DPYID CHOS
CHEN MO'I SKABS BYA GRAL TSUL KHRIMS NAG

PO ZHES DPAL LDAN BKRA SHIS SGO MANG GI RIGS PA SMRA BA'I YANG
RTZER SON PA DE NYID DANG, THOS BSAM GLING

YONGS RDZOGS CHOS GRVAR TSOGS PA'I DBUS SU DBU PHAR RNAM 'GREL
GSUM GYI DAM BCA' BZHAG  KUN MKHYEN RDO

RJE 'CHANG 'JIGS MED DBANG PO'I DRUNG NAS MDO SNGAGS KYI DBANG
LUNG SOGS MANG PO GSAN, DGUNG LO BCU

DRUG TU SON SKABS DGE RGAN GYI BKA' LTAR DRANG NGES RNAM 'BYED
KYI MTHA' DPYOD CHEN MO'I RGYUGS PHUL BAR

DGYES PA'I BKA' BSTZAL, HOR TSANG GSER KHRI RIN PO CHE'I DRUNG
NAS 'JAM DPAL ZHAL LUNG GI DMAR KHRID

SOGS DBANG LUNG 'GA' GSAN, STON CHOS CHEN MO'I SKABS JA MAR,
RTZAM PA GANG RUNG RE CHAD PA DANG, LO

GTOR RNYING PA BRDUNGS TE THUG SDOR DU 'DEBS DGOS PA SOGS KYI
SKU MNYEL BA'I SKABS SU, DGE BA'I BSHES

GNYEN RIN PO CHE NAS LTOGS SKOM LA SKYON MED, SLOB GNYER LA MA
LHOD PA GYIS, CHOS LA DKA' SPYAD BYED DGOS

PA YIN, SNGON DGON PA GSAR TSUGS KYI DUS SU GRVA PA RNAMS SA
PHUG DANG, GAS PHUG TU BZHUGS NAS DPE CHA

'DZIN SKYOR DANG, TSOGS CHOS GRVA 'GRIMS PA DANG, 'TSO BA NGAN
NGON LA BRTEN NAS DKA' SPYAD MDZAD TSUL

SOGS GSAN PAS THUGS YID 'PHROGS TE SLOB GNYER DANG, TSOGS CHOS
GRVA HUR THAG GIS 'GRIM PAR SPRO SNANG

SHIN TU 'PHEL BAR MDZAD, DPE MTSAMS LA BZHUGS NAS GRUB MTHA'
CHEN MO NYIN RER SHOG LHE LNGA RE PHAL CHER

CHAD MED THUGS SU 'DZIN, KUN MKHYEN BLA MA MCHOG GI DRUNG NAS
BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI SDOM PA MNOS, RJE BLA MA
